### [1] [Systematic Optimization of Real-Time Diffusion Model Inference on Apple M3 Ultra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16259)
*Yoichi Ochiai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文在Apple M3 Ultra上对扩散模型进行了10阶段的系统优化实验，最终通过CoreML转换与SDXS-512蒸馏模型结合3线程相机流水线，实现了512×512分辨率下22.7 FPS的实时相机img2img转换。研究发现CUDA平台的优化经验（量化加速、并行推理、Neural Engine适用性）在Apple Silicon统一内存架构上并不成立，揭示了截然不同的优化格局。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管扩散模型在NVIDIA GPU上的实时图像生成已取得快速进展，但在非CUDA平台（如Apple Silicon）上的系统优化研究极为有限，亟需探索针对该平台的优化策略。

Method: 在Apple M3 Ultra（60核GPU、512GB统一内存）上开展了10个阶段的综合优化实验，探索了CoreML转换、量化、Token Merging、Neural Engine利用、紧凑模型、帧插值、kNN搜索合成、pix2pix-turbo、光流帧跳过、知识蒸馏等多种技术，最终组合CoreML转换的蒸馏专用模型SDXS-512与3线程相机流水线。

Result: 在512×512分辨率下实现了22.7 FPS的实时相机img2img转换。

Conclusion: 系统性地证明了CUDA平台的优化经验在Apple Silicon统一内存架构上并不一定有效，揭示了包括量化无加速、并行推理无效、Neural Engine不适合大模型等截然不同的优化规律，并为Apple Silicon上的扩散模型推理提供了实用指南。

Abstract: While real-time image generation using diffusion models has advanced rapidly on NVIDIA GPUs, systematic optimization research on non-CUDA platforms such as Apple Silicon remains extremely limited. In this study, we conducted comprehensive optimization experiments across 10 phases targeting the Apple M3 Ultra (60-core GPU, 512 GB unified memory) with the goal of achieving real-time camera img2img transformation. We explored a wide range of techniques including CoreML conversion, quantization, Token Merging, Neural Engine utilization, compact model exploration, frame interpolation, kNN search-based synthesis, pix2pix-turbo, optical flow frame skipping, and knowledge distillation, quantitatively evaluating the effectiveness of each approach. Ultimately, by combining CoreML conversion of the distillation-specialized model SDXS-512 with a 3-thread camera pipeline, we achieved real-time camera img2img transformation at 22.7 FPS at 512x512 resolution. The primary contribution of this work is the systematic demonstration that optimization insights established for CUDA are not necessarily effective on Apple Silicon's unified memory architecture. We reveal an optimization landscape fundamentally different from that of NVIDIA GPUs -- including the absence of speedup from quantization, the ineffectiveness of parallel inference, and the unsuitability of the Neural Engine for large-scale models -- and provide practical guidelines for diffusion model inference on Apple Silicon.

</details>


### [2] [Reducing Credit Assignment Variance via Counterfactual Reasoning Paths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16302)
*Fei Ding,Yongkang Zhang,Yeling Peng,Youwei Wang,Guoxiong Zhou,Zijian Zeng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型多步推理中稀疏终端奖励导致的信用分配问题，提出基于反事实比较的隐式过程级优势估计方法（IBPO），将稀疏奖励转化为步骤敏感的学习信号，显著提升数学与代码推理任务的训练稳定性与性能上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习训练LLM多步推理时，稀疏终端奖励导致信用分配困难——最终反馈均匀传播至所有中间步骤，造成梯度方差大、训练不稳定、无效更新多，模型难以持续提升。

Method: 提出反事实比较的信用分配框架：对同一输入采样多条推理轨迹，利用轨迹间的差异隐式近似替代决策，构建隐式过程级优势估计器，将稀疏终端奖励转化为步骤敏感的学习信号。基于此提出隐式行为策略优化（IBPO）。

Result: 在数学和代码推理基准上，IBPO显著提升了训练稳定性和性能上限。

Conclusion: IBPO为解锁大语言模型性能潜力提供了有前景的方向，有效解决了长链推理中的信用分配难题。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning for multi-step reasoning with large language models (LLMs) often relies on sparse terminal rewards, leading to poor credit assignment conditions where the final feedback is evenly propagated across all intermediate decisions. This results in high gradient variance, unstable training, and numerous ineffective updates, ultimately causing the model to fail and preventing sustained improvement. We introduce a counterfactual comparison-based credit assignment framework, which samples multiple reasoning trajectories under the same input. By treating their differences as an implicit approximation of alternative decisions, we construct an implicit process-level advantage estimator that transforms sparse terminal rewards into step-sensitive learning signals. Based on this, we propose Implicit Behavior Policy Optimization (IBPO), which significantly improves training stability and performance upper bounds on mathematical and code reasoning benchmarks, pointing to a promising direction for unlocking the performance potential of LLMs.

</details>


### [3] [When Actions Disappear: Adversarial Action Removal in Self-Play Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16312)
*Arahan Kujur*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究自对弈强化学习中的对抗性动作屏蔽攻击——攻击者选择性移除受害者可用的合法动作。实验表明，这种攻击比随机屏蔽和扰动攻击造成更大损害，且攻击具有持久性、可迁移性，自对弈会放大攻击效果，受害者即使经过大量屏蔽训练也无法恢复。机制上，攻击者针对高价值决策点，可通过两种基于加权容量的指标（CAC$_w$和CAC$_v$）来刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索自对弈强化学习中动作可用性作为新的鲁棒性攻击面，研究通过选择性移除合法动作（而非扰动观察或动作）进行对抗攻击的效果和机制。

Method: 在扑克（6到5,531个信息状态）和非扑克领域，使用强化学习智能体（Q-learning、PPO、NFSP、神经NFSP、DQN）作为受害者，训练攻击者学习选择性屏蔽合法动作；提出reach-weighted contingent action capacity (CAC$_w$)和value-weighted refinement CAC$_v$两种指标量化攻击机制。

Result: 学习型屏蔽攻击比随机屏蔽和基于扰动的基线造成显著更大的损害；攻击跨多种算法有效并可在智能体间迁移；自对弈放大攻击效果；即使经过大量屏蔽训练，受害者也无法恢复；攻击者针对高价值决策点，CAC$_w$和CAC$_v$可有效刻画该机制。

Conclusion: 动作可用性是自对弈强化学习中一个独特的鲁棒性攻击面，值得进一步关注和防御。

Abstract: We study adversarial action masking in self-play reinforcement learning: an attacker selectively removes legal actions from a victim's action set. Unlike observation or action perturbations, removal eliminates decision options before the agent acts. Across poker games scaling from 6 to 5,531 information states and two non-poker domains, learned masking causes substantially more damage than random masking and learned perturbation baselines. The attack persists across Q-learning, PPO, NFSP, neural NFSP, and DQN victims; transfers across agents; is amplified by self-play; and shows no recovery under extended masked training. Mechanistically, the adversary targets high-value decision points, captured by reach-weighted contingent action capacity (CAC$_w$) and a value-weighted refinement CAC$_v$. These results identify action availability as a distinct robustness surface in self-play RL.

</details>


### [4] [A Structural Threshold in Decision Capacity Governs Collapse in Self-Play Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16315)
*Arahan Kujur*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究发现，在自对弈强化学习智能体中，决策能力存在一个临界阈值：当所有正向访问的偶然决策点被消除时，智能体迅速崩溃至确定性的利用吸引子（接近最大损失的固定点）；而保留哪怕一个这样的决策点即可防止崩溃。该现象源自约束下的共同适应，与时间无关、可逆，且随函数近似而加剧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究自对弈强化学习智能体在非对称规则扰动下是否会发生崩溃，以及崩溃的条件和临界点。

Method: 在多种扑克变体、矩阵博弈、骰子游戏中使用多种学习算法进行实验，通过消除所有正向访问的偶然决策点（positive-reach contingent decisions）来观察智能体行为变化，并与冻结基线和固定对手对照实验对比。

Result: 消除所有正向访问的偶然决策点导致智能体迅速收敛到确定性利用吸引子（固定点，接近最大损失）；保留至少一个这样的决策点即可防止崩溃。该现象时序不变、可逆，函数近似下更严重，且严重程度通过正向访问加权的决策能力连续缩放。

Conclusion: 自对弈强化学习中存在一个尖锐的阈值：零正向访问加权的偶然决策能力导致崩溃，而高于零则保持稳定；该机制源于约束下的共同适应而非扰动本身。

Abstract: We show that a threshold in decision capacity determines whether self-play reinforcement learning agents collapse under asymmetric rule perturbations. Across poker variants, matrix games, a dice game, and multiple learning algorithms, eliminating all positive-reach contingent decisions causes rapid convergence to a deterministic exploitation attractor, a fixed point at near-maximal loss. Preserving even a single positive-reach contingent decision point prevents this collapse. A frozen baseline and fixed-opponent control confirm that the mechanism is co-adaptation under constraint, not the perturbation itself. The phenomenon is timing-invariant, fully reversible upon action restoration, and intensifies under function approximation. These results establish a sharp threshold at zero reach-weighted contingent action capacity, with severity scaling continuously via reach-weighted capacity in the tested domains.

</details>


### [5] [Forecasting Medium-Horizon Alzheimer's Disease Progression: Residual Gap-Aware Transformers for 24-Month CDR-SB Change from ADNI Clinical and Biomarker Histories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16319)
*Ran Tong,Tong Wang,Lanruo Wang,Yin Ni*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于锚点的残差间隙感知Transformer模型，用于阿尔茨海默病中期进展预测。模型结合混合效应统计参考（含随机截距）与Transformer残差学习，通过三元组标记化处理不规则生物标志物历史，并引入可学习非负时间间隙惩罚。在ADNI数据集（2600个锚点样本）上，与线性混合效应基线、GRU-D和STraTS相比，MSE降低13.1%，预测-观测相关性提升26.4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阿尔茨海默病的中期进展预测面临两大挑战：未来临床评分与基线严重程度紧密相关，而生物标志物历史数据不规则且观测不完整。现有方法难以有效利用这些不规则时序信息进行中期预测。

Method: 1）锚定分析：以轻度认知障碍访视为锚点，定义未来18-30个月内最接近24个月的CDR-SB变化量为响应变量；2）混合效应参考模型：包含参与者层面的随机截距；3）残差间隙感知Transformer：对锚前临床和生物标志物历史进行残差学习，采用观测级三元组标记化处理不规则数据，并在自注意力中引入可学习非负时间间隙惩罚。

Result: 在5次参与者级随机划分下，所提模型在所有指标上取得最优平均测试性能：相比混合效应基线MSE降低13.1%，预测-观测相关性提升26.4%；同时优于GRU-D和STraTS的平均误差和相关性指标。

Conclusion: 统计锚定和间隙感知残差学习为阿尔茨海默病中期进展预测提供了一种有效的结构化框架。

Abstract: Medium-horizon Alzheimer's disease progression prediction is difficult because future clinical scores can remain tied to baseline severity, while biomarker histories are irregular and incompletely observed. We develop an anchor-based analysis of 24-month Clinical Dementia Rating Sum of Boxes (CDR-SB) change using harmonized Alzheimer's Disease Neuroimaging Initiative (ADNI) tables. Each labeled sample is anchored at a mild cognitive impairment visit, uses only clinical and biomarker history observed at or before that anchor, and defines the response as CDR-SB at the future visit closest to 24 months within an 18--30 month window minus anchor CDR-SB. The analytic cohort contains 2,600 labeled anchors from 858 participants and 7,276 longitudinal rows. We propose a residual gap-aware transformer that combines a mixed-effects statistical reference with transformer-based residual learning from pre-anchor clinical and biomarker histories. The model uses participant-level random intercepts in the mixed-effects reference, observation-level triplet tokenization for irregular histories, and a learned nonnegative time-gap penalty inside self-attention. We compare the proposed model with a Bayesian-information-criterion-selected linear mixed-effects baseline, GRU-D, and STraTS under repeated participant-level train--test splits. Across five participant-level random seeds, the proposed model achieves the best mean test performance across all reported metrics, reducing MSE by 13.1% and increasing prediction--observation correlation by 26.4% relative to the mixed-effects baseline. It also improves over both GRU-D and STraTS in mean error and correlation. These results show that statistical anchoring and gap-aware residual learning provide a useful structure for medium-horizon Alzheimer's disease progression prediction.

</details>


### [6] [AdaGraph: A Graph-Native Clustering Algorithm That Overcomes the Curse of Dimensionality and Enables Scientific Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16320)
*Ahmed Elmahdi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出AdaGraph，一种基于图拓扑的原生聚类算法，通过结构中心机器学习范式有效克服维度灾难，在高维数据上显著优于传统聚类方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于距离的聚类方法在高维空间中因距离度量失效而面临维度灾难，亟需一种不依赖欧氏距离、仅基于拓扑结构的聚类方法。

Method: AdaGraph完全在kNN图拓扑中运行，采用结构中心计算替代几何中心计算，结合SLCD原型-部署框架，无需预设聚类数k，自然处理噪声；使用基于拓扑的聚类有效性指标Graph-SCOPE进行无监督调优。

Result: 在10个合成基准上（d=10至5000），Graph-SCOPE平均ARI=0.900，9/10正确选择k，Kendall tau>=0.92；在肝癌基因共表达、文本聚类（20NG-6cat ARI=0.751，相对提升62%）、材料科学聚类三个领域均取得最优结果。

Conclusion: 基于图拓扑的结构中心机器学习范式能有效克服维度灾难，AdaGraph作为该范式的实例，在高维无监督学习中展现出广泛适用性和显著优势。

Abstract: We present AdaGraph, a graph-native clustering algorithm born from the Structure-Centric Machine Learning (SC-ML) paradigm -- a new field of unsupervised learning that replaces geometry-centric (distance-based) computation with structure-centric (topology-based) computation, fundamentally dissolving the curse of dimensionality. AdaGraph operates entirely within the kNN graph topology, a representation that retains meaningful relational structure in arbitrarily high dimensions where Euclidean distance metrics become uninformative. AdaGraph requires no a priori specification of the number of clusters k, handles noise natively, and scales via the SLCD (Sample-Learn-Calibrate-Deploy) prototype-deployment framework. As its unsupervised tuning objective, AdaGraph pairs with Graph-SCOPE, the topology-based cluster validity index introduced as a separate SC-ML contribution. On 10 synthetic benchmarks spanning d=10 to d=5000, Graph-SCOPE achieves mean ARI=0.900 and correctly selects k on 9/10 datasets -- outperforming Silhouette, Davies-Bouldin, and Calinski-Harabasz -- while maintaining Kendall tau >= 0.92 with ground-truth cluster quality across all dimensionalities (Silhouette: tau ~= 0.46). We validate AdaGraph across three scientific domains: (1) gene co-expression discovery in hepatocellular carcinoma (GSE14520, 10,000 genes, 488 patients, no dimensionality reduction), where AdaGraph identifies condition-specific gene modules that WGCNA, ICA, NMF, and Spectral Biclustering fail to resolve; (2) natural language text clustering, where AdaGraph achieves ARI=0.751 on 20NG-6cat versus HDBSCAN's 0.464 (62% relative improvement); (3) materials science clustering of superconductors (145-dimensional Magpie features), perovskites, and JARVIS-DFT materials, where AdaGraph achieves the highest Graph-SCOPE on all three datasets.

</details>


### [7] [Orth-Dion: Eliminating Geometric Mismatch in Distributed Low-Rank Spectral Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16341)
*Tatsuhiro Nakamori,Laura Gomezjurado Gonzalez,Ganesh Talluri,Ansh Tiwari,Hideyuki Kawashima,Ioannis Mitliagkas,Guillaume Rabusseau,Hiroki Naganuma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Orth-Dion通过QR正交化替代列归一化，以相同的通信成本实现了与全秩谱方法匹配的收敛速率，解决了Dion方法因几何不匹配导致的收敛缓慢问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Dion方法虽然通过秩r分解实现了分布式训练中的低秩梯度压缩，但其列归一化操作并未产生Muon所隐含的秩r极分解因子，导致收敛速率比全秩谱方法慢一个√r因子。这种几何不匹配也影响了平滑项和误差反馈递归分析，进而损害了经验性能。

Method: 提出Orth-Dion方法，将Dion的列归一化替换为QR正交化。在非欧几里得平滑性假设下，利用自洽不动点论证去除了误差反馈分析中常见的有界漂移假设，并采用时间平均收缩技术，要求误差序列在平均意义而非每步收缩。

Result: Orth-Dion在秩r方向曲率常数为L_r的条件下，达到O(√(L_r/T))的收敛速率，与精确谱方法匹配，且每步通信成本与Dion相同。大规模语言模型预训练实验验证了√r缩放规律，表明Orth-Dion以Dion的通信成本弥合了与Muon的收敛差距。

Conclusion: 通过纠正几何不匹配，Orth-Dion在保持通信效率的同时实现了与全秩谱方法相当的收敛性能，为低秩梯度压缩与谱优化器的结合提供了理论完备的解决方案。

Abstract: Low-rank gradient compression reduces communication in distributed training by representing updates with rank-$r$ factors. Dion is a recent method that approximates Muon, a spectral optimizer that orthogonalizes momentum, using one step of power iteration followed by column normalization (rescaling each column of the right factor to unit length). This makes it compatible with fully sharded data parallel training, but it converges more slowly than full-rank spectral methods. We show that this gap is geometric: column normalization does not yield the rank-$r$ polar factor that Muon implicitly targets, so the resulting direction violates the dual-norm constraint of the low-rank spectral geometry, and the rate picks up an extra factor of $\sqrt{r}$ even though the low-rank approximation of the gradient itself is accurate. The same mismatch enters the smoothness term and the error-feedback recursion in the analysis, which has a knock-on effect on empirical performance. We propose Orth-Dion, which replaces column normalization with QR orthogonalization of the right factor. Under non-Euclidean smoothness, with $L_r$ the curvature constant along rank-$r$ directions, Orth-Dion attains rate $O(\sqrt{L_r/T})$, matching exact spectral methods at the same per-step communication cost as Dion. The proof removes the bounded-drift assumption common in prior error-feedback analyses via a self-consistent fixed-point argument, and uses a time-averaged contraction that only requires the error sequence to contract on average rather than at every step. Experiments on large-scale language model pre-training validate the predicted $\sqrt{r}$ scaling and show that Orth-Dion closes the convergence gap to Muon at Dion's communication cost.

</details>


### [8] [Goal-Conditioned Supervised Learning for LLM Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16345)
*Shijun Li,Kaiwen Dong,Xiang Gao,Joydeep Ghosh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出目标条件监督学习（GCSL）作为LLM的离线微调框架，通过将反馈信号直接作为显式目标进行监督学习，并引入基于质量阈值的目标公式和自然语言目标表示，在无毒性生成、代码生成和推荐任务上优于标准离线微调基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM对齐方法中，在线方法（如RL）依赖外部奖励模型和迭代 rollout，成本高且难以部署；离线方法（如SFT和DPO）存在局限：SFT将分级反馈压缩为二元监督，DPO依赖难以获取的成对偏好数据。需要一种既高效又无需复杂数据要求的离线对齐方法。

Method: 提出目标条件监督学习（GCSL）框架：1）将反馈信号直接作为显式目标，通过纯监督学习训练模型生成达成该目标的响应；2）引入新型目标公式，定义学习为持续追求超越目标质量阈值的结果，而非模仿选定高质量子集的样本，以缓解SFT和经典GCSL的有界学习效应；3）提出自然语言目标表示，充分利用LLM的语义理解和推理能力。

Result: 在无毒性生成、代码生成和LLM推荐三个任务上，所提方法一致优于标准离线微调基线（如SFT、DPO），同时保留了监督学习的高效性、可扩展性和简单的数据需求。

Conclusion: 将反馈信号作为显式目标进行监督学习是一种有效的离线对齐范式，通过合理的阈值目标设计和自然语言表示，可以在保持监督学习优势的同时显著提升对齐质量。

Abstract: Large language models often require fine-tuning to better align their behavior with user intent at deployment. Existing approaches are commonly divided into online and offline paradigms. Online methods, such as RL-based alignment, can directly optimize outcome quality but typically rely on external reward models and iterative rollouts, making them costly and difficult to deploy in many cases. Offline methods are more efficient, but prevailing approaches such as supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and direct preference optimization (DPO) remain limited: SFT typically collapses graded feedback into binary supervision, while DPO depends on paired preference data that is often unavailable or expensive to construct.
  In this paper, we propose goal-conditioned supervised learning (GCSL) as an offline fine-tuning framework for LLMs. Our core idea is to treat feedback signals directly as an explicit goal and train the model, purely through supervised learning, to generate responses that achieve that goal. To better exploit graded feedback, we further introduce a novel goal formulation that defines learning as consistently pursuing outcomes above a target quality threshold, rather than imitating samples from a selected high-quality subset. This design mitigates the bounded-learning effect of SFT and classic GCSL by explicitly guiding the model to learn the directional progression of quality. We also propose natural-language goal representations to better leverage the semantic understanding and reasoning capabilities of LLMs. We evaluate our method on three tasks: non-toxic generation, code generation, and LLM for recommendation. Results show that our approach consistently outperforms standard offline fine-tuning baselines while retaining the efficiency, scalability, and simple data requirements of supervised learning.

</details>


### [9] [PropGuard: Safeguarding LLM-MAS via Propagation-Aware Exploration and Remediation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16346)
*Bingyu Yan,Xiaoming Zhang,Jinyu Hou,Chaozhuo Li,Ziyi Zhou,Xiaozhe Zhang,Litian Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PropGuard是一个面向LLM多智能体系统的传播感知防御框架，通过构建双视角时空图、GE-GRPO训练的检测器进行可疑传播子图恢复，以及源引导修复机制，在多种通信架构和攻击场景下有效降低攻击成功率并保持高任务级防御成功率。

Method: PropGuard包含三个核心组件：1) 构建双视角时空图，结合响应中心风险估计与全状态证据保留；2) 使用GE-GRPO（图增强与群体相对策略优化）训练的检查器，在风险先验引导下顺序探索全状态图，恢复紧凑的可疑传播子图；3) 通过子图感知诊断验证有害传播，并采用源引导修复纠正上游污染、重放受影响的下游交互。

Result: 在四种通信架构和五种攻击设置下的实验表明，PropGuard能持续降低攻击成功率，同时保持高任务级防御成功率，实现了良好的效果-效率权衡。

Conclusion: PropGuard通过传播感知的防御框架有效解决了LLM-MAS中的级联安全风险，在细粒度传播追踪和污染修复方面优于现有防御方法。

Abstract: LLM-based multi-agent systems (LLM-MAS) have become a promising paradigm for solving complex tasks through role specialization, tool use, memory, and collaborative reasoning. However, these interactions create new security risks that malicious instructions injected through messages, tools, or memories can propagate across agents and rounds, causing system-level compromise. Existing defenses largely rely on local filtering or graph-based anomaly detection, but they often fail to trace fine-grained propagation paths or remediate contaminated states without disrupting benign collaboration. We propose PropGuard, a propagation-aware framework for safeguarding LLM-MAS. PropGuard constructs a dual-view spatio-temporal graph that combines response-centric risk estimation with full-state evidence preservation. Guided by these risk priors, a GE-GRPO trained inspector sequentially explores the full-state graph to recover compact suspicious propagation subgraphs. PropGuard then verifies harmful propagation through subgraph-aware diagnosis and applies source-guided remediation to correct upstream contamination and replay affected downstream interactions. Experiments across four communication architectures and five attack settings demonstrate that PropGuard consistently lowers attack success while maintaining high task-level defense success, achieving a favorable effectiveness--efficiency trade-off.

### [11] [Flow-Direct: Feedback-Efficient and Reusable Guidance for Flow Models via Non-Parametric Guidance Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16348)
*Kim Yong Tan,Yueming Lyu,Ivor Tsang,Yew-Soon Ong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Flow-Direct通过持久性引导场（基于所有历史奖励评估样本构建的非参数估计器）实现反馈高效且可重用的无训练扩散/流模型引导，理论推导自基础分布与奖励加权目标分布之间的对数密度比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无训练引导方法仅在局部梯度近似或离散搜索决策中短暂使用奖励反馈，随后丢弃，导致反馈效率低下。

Method: 提出Flow-Direct框架，通过持久性引导场引导生成过程。该场理论上从基础分布与奖励加权目标分布的对数密度比解析推导，实践中作为非参数估计器，由所有累积的奖励评估样本构建。

Result: Flow-Direct具有高反馈效率（每个评估样本都用于优化全局引导场，不浪费奖励信息）和自然可重用性（优化完成后，收集的数据集定义可重用的引导场，无需额外奖励评估即可生成新目标样本；不同引导场可组合生成满足多目标的样本）。

Conclusion: Flow-Direct通过持久性引导场解决了现有无训练引导方法反馈效率低下的问题，同时实现了引导场的可重用与多目标组合能力。

Abstract: Training-free guidance enables pre-trained diffusion and flow models to optimize application-specific objectives using feedback from external black-box reward functions. However, existing methods are feedback-inefficient because reward feedback is used only transiently to inform a localized gradient approximation or a discrete search decision, and is subsequently discarded. To address this limitation, we propose Flow-Direct, a framework that guides the generation process via a persistent guidance field. Theoretically, this guidance field is analytically derived from the log-density ratio between the base and reward-weighted target distributions; it transports the pre-trained distribution to the target distribution. In practice, the field is implemented as a non-parametric estimator constructed from all accumulated reward-evaluated samples. As more samples are collected during optimization, this empirical guidance field becomes increasingly accurate. This persistent formulation yields two major advantages. First, Flow-Direct is highly feedback-efficient: because every evaluated sample is used to refine the global guidance field, no reward information is wasted. Second, the framework is naturally reusable: once optimization is complete, the collected dataset defines a reusable guidance field for generating novel target samples without additional reward evaluations, and distinct guidance fields can be combined to generate samples that simultaneously satisfy multiple objectives.

### [12] [Geometric Asymmetry in MoE Specialization: Functional Decorrelation and Representational Overlap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16349)
*Feilong Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过Jacobian-PCA-Grassmann统一框架分析MoE层，发现专家功能去相关与表示子空间重叠共存，且路由稀疏性是形成这种几何结构的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MoE架构通过稀疏路由实现可扩展容量，但专家专业化的几何结构仍缺乏深入理解，需要统一的分析框架来揭示其内在机制。

Method: 提出Jacobian-PCA-Grassmann统一框架，在函数空间和表示空间两个层面分析MoE层；在Mistral、Qwen等预训练MoE Transformer上进行实证研究，并设计可控路由实验（对比top-k路由与全软路由）。

Result: 发现一致性结构不对称性：专家间雅可比对齐度持续低（接近零），即功能去相关；而路由表示占据不同但部分重叠的子空间。Top-k路由导致更尖锐的功能分离和更大的子空间散度，全软路由则产生更纠缠的专家结构。

Conclusion: MoE层可被视为在共享表示流形上的重叠子流形上实现局部去相关算子，路由稀疏性是塑造该几何结构的关键因素，该框架为研究现代Transformer中的条件计算提供了通用诊断工具。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures achieve scalable capacity through sparse routing, yet the geometric structure of expert specialization remains poorly understood. We introduce a unified Jacobian-PCA-Grassmann framework for analyzing MoE layers in both function space and representation space. Across pretrained MoE Transformers (Mistral, Qwen), we find a consistent structural asymmetry: experts exhibit strong functional decorrelation (consistently low, near-zero cross-expert Jacobian alignment) while their routed representations occupy distinct but partially overlapping subspaces. This indicates that functional decorrelation and representation overlap coexist rather than coincide in MoE specialization. Controlled routing experiments further indicate that routing sparsity appears to be a key factor shaping this geometry: top-k routing induces sharper functional separation and larger subspace divergence, whereas fully soft routing yields more entangled expert structure. Together, these results suggest a geometric interpretation in which MoE layers may be viewed as implementing locally decorrelated operators over overlapping submanifolds on a shared representation manifold, and provide a general diagnostic framework for studying conditional computation in modern Transformer architectures.

### [14] [S-Bus: Automatic Read-Set Reconstruction for Multi-Agent LLM State Coordination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17076)
*Sajjad Khan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: S-Bus是一个HTTP中间件，通过服务端DeliveryLog机制实现可观测读隔离（ORI），在无需修改Agent SDK的情况下自动检测并防止多Agent协作中的结构性竞态条件（写-写冲突和跨分片脏读），经TLAPS形式化验证、TLC模型检测和Dafny归纳论证，与PostgreSQL SERIALIZABLE和Redis WATCH/MULTI达到同等预防效果，但ORI在单分片协作写入场景下可能传播矛盾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有并发LLM Agent共享可变自然语言状态时会产生结构性竞态条件（SRC），即写-写冲突和跨分片脏读会静默破坏Agent输出。而主流多Agent框架（LangGraph、CrewAI、AutoGen）缺乏对共享状态的写所有权语义，无法解决此问题。

Method: 提出S-Bus HTTP中间件，核心机制是服务端DeliveryLog：每个Agent维护一个HTTP GET操作日志，在提交时自动重建Agent读集，无需修改Agent SDK（基于HTTP/1.1）。DeliveryLog提供可观测读隔离（ORI）——一种在HTTP可观测投影上的部分因果一致性，防止通过共享分片协作时的结构性竞态条件。通过三层机械化证据验证：TLAPS机器检查ReadSetSoundness和ORICommitSafety（保留一个类型公理）、TLC在N=3下穷举搜索20,763,484个状态无违规、Dafny证明9个归纳正确性引理。

Result: （1）形式化验证通过；（2）在427,308个HTTP-409冲突的共享分片竞争扫描中，与PostgreSQL 17 SERIALIZABLE和Redis 7 WATCH/MULTI达到零Type-I损坏的同等预防效果；（3）ORI的运行范围具有拓扑条件性：在专用分片工作负载中语义中立，但在单分片协作写入中因保留传播并发矛盾而产生有害影响。

Conclusion: S-Bus通过DeliveryLog和ORI在HTTP层面有效解决了多Agent共享状态的结构性竞态条件，无需修改Agent内部实现，形式化验证和实证结果均支持其有效性，但需注意其局限性：在单分片协作写入场景下可能有害。

Abstract: Concurrent LLM agents sharing mutable natural-language state produce Structural Race Conditions (SRCs): write-write and cross-shard stale-read conflicts that silently corrupt agent output. Existing multi-agent frameworks (LangGraph, CrewAI, AutoGen) provide no write-ownership semantics over shared state.
  We present S-Bus, an HTTP middleware whose central mechanism is a server-side DeliveryLog: a per-agent log of HTTP GET operations that automatically reconstructs each agent's read set at commit time without agent SDK changes under HTTP/1.1. The consistency property the DeliveryLog provides -- Observable-Read Isolation (ORI), a partial causal consistency over the HTTP-observable projection of the read set -- prevents structural race conditions when agents collaborate via shared shards.
  Three contributions: (C1) The DeliveryLog mechanism for automatic HTTP-traffic-based read-set reconstruction, with three-tier mechanised evidence: ReadSetSoundness and ORICommitSafety machine-checked in TLAPS (modulo one retained typing axiom); exhaustive TLC at N=3 (20,763,484 distinct states, zero violations); Dafny discharges 9 inductive soundness lemmas. (C2) Empirical structural-conflict prevention parity against PostgreSQL 17 SERIALIZABLE and Redis 7 WATCH/MULTI on shared-shard contention sweeps with 427,308 active HTTP-409 conflicts: zero Type-I corruptions across all three backends. (C3) ORI's operating envelope is topology-conditional: semantically neutral in dedicated-shard workloads; harmful in single-shard collaborative writing because preservation propagates concurrent contradictions.
  Source code: https://github.com/sajjadanwar0/sbus

</details>


### [15] [Augmenting Human Evaluation with LLM Judges: How Many Human Reviews Do You Need?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16354)
*Jane Paik Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出将LLM评估者从替代人类评价的角色转变为辅助角色，并采用两阶段抽样设计（第一阶段LLM评估所有样本，第二阶段人类评估子样本），利用双重稳健估计量进行统计推断，同时给出了样本量确定和实验设计优化的方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出两阶段抽样设计：第一阶段对所有观测使用LLM评估，第二阶段对子样本收集人类评分；采用缺失数据文献中的双重稳健估计量（利用缺失模型已知的特性）；基于估计量的渐近方差推导样本量确定方法以达成目标统计功效；提出通过增加人类评分在LLM预测性不高的评估类型中的比例来优化实验设计。

Conclusion: LLM评估者应作为人类评价的辅助而非替代，本文提供了正规统计框架来设计人机协作评估实验，填补了关于保留多少人类监督的指导空白。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used as automated evaluators of AI systems, including in high-stakes applications. In this role, LLMs are used to generate judgments about the quality, appropriateness, or even safety of model outputs. This approach is motivated by practical constraints. Expert human ratings are costly and difficult to scale, whereas LLM ratings can be produced quickly at low cost. However, current approaches to deploying LLM evaluators are ad hoc, typically limited to reporting agreement metrics between human and LLM judges as a justification for substitution of human ratings, and lack a formal basis for study design. This paper (1) shifts the role of the LLM judge from substitutive to auxiliary, and (2) formulates the LLM-as-a-judge paradigm as one of augmenting human evaluation through a two-stage sampling design, where LLM evaluations are measured for all observations at the first stage and human ratings are partially observed for a subsample at the second stage. We propose to use a doubly robust estimator from the missing data literature, which takes advantage of the robustness property against the prediction model, since the missingness model is known by design. Using the asymptotic variance of this estimator, we propose how sample sizes of human and LLM ratings can be determined to achieve a targeted level of power. We also show that a study can be efficiently designed by allocating more human ratings for types of evaluations where the predictability of LLM ratings is not high. To the best of our knowledge, there is very little guidance on how much human oversight should be retained when validating benchmarks.

### [16] [OSCAR: Offline Spectral Covariance-Aware Rotation for 2-bit KV Cache Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17757)
*Zhongzhu Zhou,Donglin Zhuang,Jisen Li,Ziyan Chen,Shuaiwen Leon Song,Ben Athiwaratkun,Xiaoxia Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OSCAR是一种面向长上下文LLM服务的超低位KV缓存量化方法，通过估计注意力感知的协方差结构来推导固定旋转和裁剪阈值，实现INT2量化且保持精度，同时设计了兼容现代LLM服务框架的自定义INT2注意力内核，在Qwen3和GLM-4等模型上验证了其有效性，实现了约8倍内存压缩和最高7倍吞吐提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: INT2 KV缓存量化对长上下文LLM服务具有吸引力，但现有方法（如Hadamard变换这种简单旋转）虽然能减少离群值，由于未与下游注意力对齐，在INT2精度下仍会出现显著退化，难以同时实现高精度和可部署性。

Method: 提出OSCAR方法，离线估计注意力感知的协方差结构，并据此推导固定的旋转矩阵和裁剪阈值，使KV量化与注意力实际消费的协方差结构对齐；同时开发了自定义INT2注意力内核，兼容分页KV缓存服务和融合内核流水线，可无缝集成到SGLang和vLLM等框架中。

Result: 在Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507和Qwen3-8B上，OSCAR将BF16精度差距缩小至3.78和1.42个点（朴素旋转INT2几乎崩溃）；在Qwen3-32B和GLM-4（358B参数）上表现与BF16相当；在128K长上下文RULER-NIAH任务中保持鲁棒；实现约8倍KV缓存压缩，相同内存预算下吞吐提升最高7倍，batch-size-1解码速度提升最高3倍。

Conclusion: OSCAR通过注意力感知的协方差对齐方法有效解决了INT2 KV缓存量化的精度退化问题，并在大规模模型和长上下文中验证了其有效性和可部署性，为超低位KV缓存量化在工业级LLM服务系统中的实际应用提供了可行方案。

Abstract: INT2 KV-cache quantization is attractive for long-context LLM serving, but it remains difficult to make both accurate and deployable. Simple rotations such as Hadamard transforms reduce outliers, but still degrade at INT2 because they are not aligned with downstream attention. We propose OSCAR, an Ultra-low-bit KV Cache quantization method that estimates attention-aware covariance structures offline and uses them to derive fixed rotations and clipping thresholds for quantization. In this way, it aligns KV quantization with the covariance structures that attention actually consumes. More importantly, we not only provide theoretical justification but also develop a fully deployable OSCAR system with a custom INT2 attention kernel that remains compatible with paged KV-cache serving and fused kernel pipelines, enabling seamless integration into modern LLM serving frameworks such as SGLang and vLLM.
  We evaluate our methods on recent reasoning models with reasoning traces of up to 32k tokens across 5 tasks. On Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507 and Qwen3-8B, OSCAR reduces the BF16 accuracy gap to 3.78 and 1.42 points, respectively, while naive rotation INT2 collapses to nearly zero. We further scale OSCAR to Qwen3-32B and GLM-4.7 (358B params), where it remains effectively on par with BF16. On long context - RULER-NIAH up to 128K, OSCAR remains robust on both Qwen3 models, while naive rotation INT2 collapses. System-wise, OSCAR reduces KV-cache memory by approximately 8x, improves throughput by up to 7x at large batch sizes under the same memory budget, and accelerates batch-size-1 decoding by up to 3x over BF16 due to reduced memory bandwidth overhead.

</details>


### [17] [TailedTS: Benchmark Dataset for Heavy-Tailed Time Series Prediction and Periodicity Quantification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16361)
*Xinyu Chen,HanQin Cai,Lijun Ding,Jinhua Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出TailedTS，一个基于2024年维基百科每小时页面浏览量构建的大规模基准数据集，包含约246.9亿数据点，专门用于测试时间序列预测模型在重尾、零膨胀和非高斯条件下的表现。实验发现高频页面周期性结构显著弱于低频页面，且标准高斯估计器在高流量类别上表现退化，而鲁棒替代方法在所有流量尺度上均有一致提升。

Motivation: 现有时间序列基准（如M4、M5、UCI电力数据集）缺乏对重尾分布、零膨胀和非高斯特征的充分覆盖，难以评估模型在极端波动下的鲁棒性。作者希望通过维基百科流量的幂律分布特性，构建一个自然且严苛的测试环境。

Method: 从2024年全年维基百科每小时页面浏览量中提取数据，涵盖约300万独立页面/月，以Apache Parquet格式存储。引入基于稀疏自回归（带稀疏性和非负性约束）的周期性量化框架；在非高斯损失函数族（ℓ1范数、Huber、分位数、ℓp范数）下进行标准化预测基准评估。

Abstract: We present TailedTS, a large-scale benchmark dataset derived from Wikipedia hourly page view observations throughout 2024, specifically designed to test time series forecasting models under heavy-tailed, zero-inflated, and non-Gaussian conditions. The dataset comprises approximately 24.69 billion data points spanning roughly 3 million unique Wikipedia pages per month, stored in high-efficiency Apache Parquet format. Wikipedia traffic follows a pronounced power-law distribution where roughly 5% of pages account for over 70% of total page views, creating a natural and rigorous testbed for model robustness against extreme volatility that are absent from or underrepresented in existing benchmarks such as M4, M5, and UCI electricity datasets. TailedTS enables several research tasks. First, we introduce a periodicity quantification framework based on sparse autoregression with sparsity and non-negativity constraints, revealing that frequently-viewed pages exhibit significantly weaker periodic structure than their less-viewed counterparts, showing direct implications for server allocation and traffic forecasting on large digital platforms. Second, we provide standardized prediction benchmarks evaluated under a suite of non-Gaussian loss functions, including $\ell_1$-norm, Huber, quantile, and $\ell_p$-norm losses, demonstrating that standard Gaussian-based estimators degrade substantially on high-volume page categories, while robust alternatives provide consistent gains across all traffic scales. TailedTS is publicly available at https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.17070469.

### [18] [When Is Rank-1 Steering Cheap? Geometry, Granularity, and Budgeted Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16362)
*John T. Robertson,Jianing Zhu,Haris Vikalo,Zhangyang Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出激活转向（Activation Steering）的困难主要源于搜索难度而非概念本身不可用秩一表示。通过引入基于几何引导的搜索方法、概念粒度（Concept Granularity）度量以及GRACE框架，显著降低了有效干预的搜索成本，并揭示了何时秩一干预是廉价且稳定的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作发现激活转向在不同概念上效果差异显著，常将此归因于许多概念无法被单一转向方向捕获。本文认为这种差异很大程度上反映了搜索困难（search difficulty），而非概念本身的不可表示性——有用的秩一干预往往存在，但找到它的成本很高。

Method: (1) 将秩一转向形式化为预算约束下的干预层与系数优化问题；(2) 发现提示边界方向对齐（prompt-boundary directional alignment）可预测有效干预位置，提出几何引导搜索；(3) 引入概念粒度（Concept Granularity）度量，衡量对比上下文间方向异质性；(4) 提出GRACE框架，利用激活几何诊断转向困难来源、选择补救措施并高效分配优化资源。

Result: 几何引导搜索在三个模型族上平均减少39.8%的试验次数即可达到95%的最优效用。概念粒度与收敛速度（r=0.44, p<0.001）和最优性能（r=-0.46, p<0.001）显著相关。GRACE框架实现了从诊断到干预的端到端优化。

Conclusion: 本文将问题从"秩一何时失败"转向"秩一何时廉价且稳定"，将激活几何从描述性工具转变为LLM控制的可操作先验知识。

Abstract: Activation steering offers a lightweight way to control LLMs without retraining, but its effectiveness varies sharply across concepts. Prior work often reads this variability as evidence that many concepts are not captured by a single steering direction. We argue instead that much of it reflects search difficulty: a useful rank-1 intervention often exists, but finding it can be expensive.
  We formalize rank-1 steering as a budget-constrained optimization over intervention layer and coefficient. Across concepts and model families, prompt-boundary directional alignment predicts where effective interventions occur, enabling geometry-guided search that reaches high utility with substantially fewer evaluations, reducing the trials needed to recover 95\% of best-found utility by 39.8\% on average across three model families. To explain why some concepts remain expensive even under better search, we introduce \emph{concept granularity}, a measure of directional heterogeneity across contrastive contexts. Granularity distinguishes concepts whose difference vectors share a stable global direction from those where prompts agree locally within each input but the utility-maximizing direction rotates systematically across inputs. Higher granularity is associated with slower convergence and lower best-found performance (Pearson $r{=}0.44$ with trials-to-95\%, $r{=}{-}0.46$ with best-found utility, both $p<0.001$).
  We present \textit{GRACE}, a Granularity- and Representation-Aware Concept Engineering framework that uses activation geometry to diagnose the dominant source of steering difficulty, select the appropriate remedy, and allocate optimization effort efficiently. Our results shift the frame from ``\textit{when does rank-1 fail?}'' to ``\textit{when is rank-1 cheap and stable?}'', turning activation geometry from a descriptive tool into an actionable prior for LLM control.

Effective intervention thus requires anticipating scams before the intent becomes explicit. In this paper, we propose \textbf{ORACLE} Online Reasoning for Anticipating Cross-temporal Latent thrEats, the first agentic framework for early scam anticipation from \textit{streaming app-usage} trajectories. To support this setting, we curate a real-world long-horizon benchmark of streaming app-usage trajectories, covering 12 scam types, spanning extended periods (15 days on average), involving diverse applications (95 apps), and interleaving normal and scam behaviors. To address fragmented evidence, we introduce a self-evolving context manager that adaptively consolidates entity-centric interactions over time, enabling more effective reconstruction of cross-temporal evidence from partial observations. To enhance sensitivity to latent early-stage signals, we propose an on-policy self-distillation scheme in which a teacher model, conditioned on summarized anti-scam reflections and clues by skills, supervises a student model without access to such reflections. This scheme thereby distills evidence-informed knowledge and improves recognition of emerging fraud patterns from partial trajectories. ### [22] [Mixing Times of Glauber Dynamics on Masked Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16378)
*Suvadip Sana,Sami Wolf,Neer Mehta,Alina Shah,Aitzaz Shaikh,Janna Goodman,Lionel Levine*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了掩码语言模型（MLM）在迭代生成时产生的全局分布行为。通过将迭代掩码令牌重采样建模为Glauber动力学马尔可夫链，作者发现MLM条件概率本质上是不兼容的（通过矩形测试验证），并证明了在高温下链以O(n log n)时间混合，而在低温下由于均匀局部边缘条件出现亚稳态，导致指数级慢的逃逸。实验验证了温度与序列长度相关的相变，并通过语义轨迹识别了持久结构（长寿命陷阱、循环语义盆地），以政治内容为案例进行了分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MLM定义的局部条件分布通常不对应任何一致的序列联合分布，这引发了一个根本性问题：当这些条件分布被迭代用于生成时，会产生怎样的全局分布行为？作者旨在揭示这一理论基础上的空白。

Method: 将迭代掩码令牌重采样建模为Glauber动力学马尔可夫链；提出矩形测试来检验MLM条件概率的不兼容性；在理论上分析马尔可夫链的混合时间（高温下的O(n log n)收缩结果与低温下的亚稳态指数级慢逃逸）；通过经验实验验证温度与序列长度相关的相变现象。

Result: MLM条件概率在本质上不兼容（矩形测试验证）；高温下链的混合时间为O(n log n)；低温下出现亚稳态，逃逸呈指数级慢；经验上观察到温度与序列长度相关的相变；发现了长寿命陷阱和循环语义盆地等持久语义结构。

Conclusion: MLM的迭代生成行为可通过Glauber动力学马尔可夫链进行理论刻画，其混合行为存在高温快速混合与低温亚稳态之间的相变，且稳态分布中存在可识别的语义结构（包括政治内容等敏感领域的持久模式）。

Abstract: Masked language models (MLMs) define local conditional distributions over tokens but do not, in general, correspond to any consistent joint distribution over sequences. This raises a fundamental question: what global distributional behavior is induced when such conditionals are used iteratively for generation? We address this question by modeling iterative masked-token resampling as a Glauber dynamics Markov chain on the discrete space of token sequences. We first show that MLM conditionals are intrinsically incompatible: we introduce a rectangle test that certifies this incompatibility and empirically verify its prevalence across modern MLMs. We then provide a theoretical analysis of the induced Markov chain. Under bounded cross-token influence, we establish a high-temperature contraction result implying $O(n\log n)$ mixing time where $n$ is the sequence length. In contrast, we prove that under a uniform local margin condition, the chain exhibits metastability, with exponentially slow escape from semantic basins at low temperatures. Empirically, we demonstrate a phase transition in mixing behavior as a function of temperature and sequence length, consistent with the theoretical predictions. We further characterize the induced stationary behavior through semantic trajectories, identifying persistent structures such as long-lived traps and recurrent semantic basins, with political content serving as a measurable case study.

### [23] [An Information-Theoretic Criterion for Efficient Data Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16379)
*Hanyu Li,Zhengqi Sun,Xiaotie Deng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从信息论视角解释合成数据在LLM训练中的不一致性：只有当生成-训练回路是信息开放的（依赖外部信号注入任务相关信息）时，合成数据才能提升模型性能；信息封闭回路（仅依赖模型自身输出）因数据处理不等式必然导致信息衰减和模型崩溃。此外，监督的元层级（如粗粒度二值正确性信号）决定了泛化能力与效率，并提出了学习会优先收敛到信息效率最高的信号成分这一核心论点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 合成数据在大语言模型训练中被广泛使用，但其效果高度不一致，缺乏一个统一的理论框架来解释何时有效、何时失效。

Method: 采用信息论分析方法，通过"信息开放回路"与"信息封闭回路"的二分法，结合数据处理不等式，从理论上推导合成数据有效性的边界条件。同时引入监督元层级的概念，分析不同粒度信号对泛化和效率的影响。

Result: 1) 信息封闭回路必然导致任务相关信息减少和模型崩溃；2) 信息开放回路中，粗粒度二值信号（如正确性）比细粒度信号具有更好的跨任务域泛化能力；3) 学习倾向于优先收敛到信息效率最高的信号成分，这既能加速学习，也会导致奖励破解。

Conclusion: 提出了一个统一的信息论框架来理解合成数据的有效性，为设计更可靠的合成数据生成策略提供了理论指导，并揭示了奖励破解现象的信息论根源。

Abstract: Synthetic data becomes crucial for large language model training, but its effectiveness is highly inconsistent. We provide an information-theoretic account of this inconsistency: synthetic data improves a model only when the generation-training loop is information-open, i.e., shaped by external signals (verifiers, environments, or rubrics) that inject task-relevant information beyond the model's current distribution. When the loop is information-closed (relying on the model's own outputs without such signals), the data processing inequality ensures that task-relevant information can only decrease, making collapse a predicted outcome. Among information-open pipelines, both efficiency and generalization hinge on the meta-level of supervision: a coarser signal such as binary correctness treats all acceptable outputs as equivalent, so the behavior it teaches is not tied to any particular domain or surface form and generalizes naturally across tasks and domains. These observations lead to a guiding thesis: learning preferentially converges to the most information-efficient signal component available, which accelerates learning when that component is the intended one, but causes reward hacking when a spurious pattern happens to be simpler.

### [24] [ReTAMamba: Reliability-Aware Temporal Aggregation with Mamba for Irregular Clinical Time Series Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16380)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法使用观测掩码和时间间隔信息，但未能连续捕捉历史观测的衰减可靠性，也未能在聚合过程中将多分辨率信息组织到连贯的时序上下文中。

Method: 1) 将临床时间序列重构为时间可变token序列；2) 从缺失性和经过时间估计观测可靠性；3) 用统计描述符增强区间摘要；4) Chronological Weaving整合短长期时序信息；5) 预算token路由器约束序列长度并保留信息摘要。

Result: MIMIC-IV、eICU和PhysioNet 2012上AUPRC分别相对提升7.51%、7.80%和10.15%；动态信号（心率、血压）的衰减常数比静态信号（实验室检验）大24.3%。

Conclusion: 有效预测不规则临床时间序列需要建模不仅观测了什么，还包括何时以及如何观测，即信息新鲜度和观测及时性。

Abstract: Clinical time-series data are difficult to model with methods designed for regular sequences because they exhibit irregular sampling, frequent missing values, and heterogeneous observation patterns across variables. Existing approaches commonly use observation masks and time-gap information, but they do not continuously capture the decaying reliability of past observations or consistently organize multi-resolution information within a coherent temporal context during aggregation. To address these limitations, we propose Reliability-aware Temporal Aggregation with Mamba (ReTAMamba), which reconstructs clinical time series as time-variable token sequences, estimates observation reliability from missingness and elapsed time, and augments interval summaries with statistical descriptors. Chronological Weaving is used to integrate short- and long-term temporal information within a coherent temporal context, and a budgeted token router is applied to constrain sequence length while preserving informative summaries. Experiments on MIMIC-IV, eICU, and PhysioNet 2012 show that ReTAMamba consistently improves AUPRC over strong baselines, with average relative gains of 7.51%, 7.80%, and 10.15%, respectively. Cohort-level and patient-level analyses on eICU further showed that the learned mean decay for more dynamic signals, such as heart rate and blood pressure, was 24.3% larger than that for relatively static signals, such as laboratory test variables. These findings suggest that effective prediction in irregular clinical time series requires modeling not only what was measured, but also when and how it was observed, including information freshness and observation timeliness.

### [25] [QuantFPFlow: Quantum Amplitude Estimation for Fokker--Planck Policy Optimisation in Continuous Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16429)
*Abraham Itzhak Weinberg*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了QuantFPFlow框架，将量子振幅估计集成到随机策略优化的Fokker-Planck公式中，实现经典$\mathcal{O}(1/\varepsilon^2)$到量子$\mathcal{O}(1/\varepsilon)$的加速，并在连续控制任务上比SAC更频繁地发现全局最优解，同时保持策略熵稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典连续空间强化学习在估计Fokker-Planck配分函数时面临$\mathcal{O}(1/\varepsilon^2)$的计算成本，且易陷入局部最优。作者希望通过量子振幅估计实现二次加速，并利用FP扩散匹配机制防止策略过早收敛。

Method: 将量子振幅估计(QAE)集成到Fokker-Planck公式中，用Grover放大实现$\mathcal{O}(1/\varepsilon)$的配分函数估计；基于估计的稳态分布$\rho^*$设计探索奖励$R_{aug}=R_{env}+\alpha\log(1/\rho^*(s))$，引导智能体探索全局最优区域；通过FP扩散匹配约束策略方差。

Result: 在连续控制任务上，QuantFPFlow平均奖励1295.7±423.2 vs SAC的1284.0±474.0；全局最优发现频率33.9% vs 30.7%；策略熵维持在~6.5 nats而SAC降至1.5 nats；计算扩展性$\mathcal{O}(d^{0.35})$ vs $\mathcal{O}(d^{0.76})$。

Conclusion: QuantFPFlow通过量子启发的FP扩散匹配有效防止策略过早收敛，更频繁地发现全局最优，且计算复杂度在维度扩展上更具优势。

Abstract: We introduce \textbf{QuantFPFlow}, a reinforcement learning framework that integrates quantum amplitude estimation into the Fokker--Planck~(FP) formulation of stochastic policy optimisation. Classical continuous-space RL agents must estimate the FP partition function $Z = \int e^{-V(\mathbf{x})/D}\,d\mathbf{x}$ at cost $\calO(1/\varepsilon^{2})$; QuantFPFlow replaces this with a Grover-amplified amplitude estimator achieving $\calO(1/\varepsilon)$ -- a provable quadratic speedup. While the full quantum acceleration requires fault-tolerant hardware, the quantum-inspired classical simulation demonstrated here already exhibits the $\calO(1/\varepsilon)$ algorithmic structure.
  The estimated stationary distribution $\rhostar$ drives a theoretically grounded exploration bonus $\Raug = \Renv + α\log(1/\rhostar(s))$. This bonus steers the agent toward globally optimal regions of multimodal reward landscapes while simultaneously constraining policy variance through FP diffusion matching.
  On a continuous-control task specifically designed to expose local-optima failure, QuantFPFlow achieves mean reward $1{,}295.7 \pm 423.2$ versus $1{,}284.0 \pm 474.0$ for Soft Actor-Critic~(SAC), while discovering the global optimum \textbf{10.4\,\% more frequently} (33.9\,\% vs.\ 30.7\,\%). Policy entropy remains near $H(π)\approx 6.5$\,nats throughout training, whereas SAC collapses to $1.5$\,nats, confirming that FP diffusion matching actively prevents premature convergence. Dimensionality experiments further show computational scaling of $\calO(d^{0.35})$ for QuantFPFlow versus $\calO(d^{0.76})$ for classical FP estimation.

### [26] [A Theory of Training Profit-Optimal LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16430)
*Sophie Hao,William Merrill*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过结合规模定律与微观经济学理论，构建了LLM训练企业的经济模型，分析在计算受限和数据受限两种场景下，模型规模、训练预算与利润最大化之间的关系，并评估了当前行业训练支出趋势的经济合理性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然已知扩大LLM规模能提升模型质量，但质量提升如何转化为潜在收入、收入增长能否抵消大规模训练和推理的成本尚不清楚，现有研究缺乏从经济理性角度对LLM训练决策的理论分析。

Method: 将规模定律与微观经济学理论结合，建立LLM训练企业的利润最大化模型。模型中LLM质量随参数量和训练token增加而提升，消费者根据质量阈值决定是否采用。分别在计算受限和数据受限两种场景下求解最优模型规模、token预算和训练支出。

Result: 计算受限下，最优模型规模和token预算与硬件效率E（FLOPs/$）呈近线性关系，训练成本随E次二次增长；数据效率提升激励更大模型和更高支出。数据受限下，利润最优训练支出与数据量D的平方成正比、与硬件效率E成反比。当前行业趋势在计算受限模式下与模型预测一致，但在数据受限或假设硬件进步停滞时并非利润最优。

Conclusion: 本文提供了利润最优的LLM训练理论，为批判性审视行业声明和长期经济决策提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Scaling LLMs requires tremendous computational resources, and recent advances in AI have gone hand in hand with massive amounts of capital expenditure. While it is established that scaling up LLMs reliably increases model quality (quantified in terms of loss or downstream evaluations), it is unclear how these quality improvements translate to potential revenue, and whether revenue increases would offset costs of larger-scale training and inference. In this work, we develop an economic model for characterizing the rational behavior of an LLM training firm by combining scaling laws with microeconomic theory. Under our model of firm behavior, LLM quality can be increased with more parameters and training tokens, leading to more potential adoption by consumers, who each have a quality threshold for using the LLM. On the other hand, additional parameters and training tokens both incur additional costs. We analyze the profit maximization problem for this model under compute-bound and data-bound regimes. In the compute-bound regime, optimal model size and token budget track hardware efficiency $E$ (FLOPs/\$) at a near-linear rate; total training cost then scales sub-quadratically in $E$. Data efficiency improvements incentivize larger models and training expenditure. When we are limited to $D$ data, profit-optimal training expenditure scales as $D^2/E$, i.e, increase with data and decreases with hardware efficiency (as well as data efficiency). Finally, we analyze practical trends in training expenditure: current trends are consistent with our most permissive model variants in the compute-bound regime, but are not profit-optimal in the data-bound regime or assuming hardware advances will stall. Overall, our results provide a theory of profit-optimal LLM training, providing a foundation for engaging critically with industry statements and supporting long-term economic decision making.

Abstract: Task allocation in smart manufacturing systems needs to operate under decentralized decision-making, dynamic workloads, and shared resource constraints. ### [29] [Byzantine-Resilient Federated Learning via QUBO-Based Client Selection on Quantum Annealers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16438)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 将客户端选择重构为QUBO问题，用量子退火器全局优化选择相互距离最近的m个客户端；2) 提出MultiSignal集成框架，基于欧氏距离和余弦Krum分数差距的双特征路由门将攻击分为四类，对规避攻击采用怀疑惩罚的QUBO加共识投票机制。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) trains a global model across decentralized clients while preserving data privacy, but at scale it is vulnerable to malicious updates. Byzantine-resilient aggregation methods such as MultiKrum score gradients against their nearest neighbors and can miss malicious updates that preserve the statistical properties of honest ones. We propose a quantum annealing approach that reformulates client selection as a Quadratic Unconstrained Binary Optimization (QUBO) problem, encoding pairwise distances into a cost function solved by quantum annealers (QA). Unlike MultiKrum's greedy per-client scoring, the QUBO formulation jointly optimizes over all subsets to find the mutually closest group of $m$ clients. At small scale (15 clients), QUBO outperforms MultiKrum on the most challenging Byzantine attacks: e.g., Advanced LIE is detected with 95.11% accuracy versus 81.33% on MNIST and 97.78% versus 75.56% on CIFAR-10. QUBO fares poorly on simpler attacks where MultiKrum excels, so the two methods are complementary. QUBO quality also degrades as the number of clients grows. To address this, we introduce a MultiSignal ensemble that uses a dual-feature routing gate based on Euclidean and cosine Krum score gaps to classify attacks into four regimes and routes evasion attacks to a suspicion-penalized QUBO with agreement voting. At 100 clients on MNIST, MultiSignal achieves 95.3% average detection accuracy versus 91.8% for classical MultiKrum, with the largest gains on Sparse Lie (72.0% to 95.2%, +23.2 points) and Advanced Lie (80.4% to 85.2%, +4.8 points). On Adult and COMPAS, it yields non-degenerate operating points competitive with the empirical static-$λ$ frontier; on ACSIncome, it preserves utility with a wider fairness-utility spread. Relative to OPDA-lite, the full controller mainly shifts the operating point toward higher utility on ACSIncome, while Adult highlights the fairness-utility trade-off between the two variants. These results position OPDA as a calibration-free controller for non-degenerate operating points in tabular fair SSL without per-dataset tuning.

TL;DR: 本文提出一种嵌套式预测框架，通过未来宏观区域趋势引导微观预测，利用谱聚类构建语义一致区域以滤除噪声，并采用渐进式粗到细预测器集成特征，在多个高维数据集上超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有时空预测方法主要依赖历史空间先验，无法捕捉不断变化的时间相关性，且在噪声和非平稳条件下存在系统性误差，难以捕获可靠的交互关系。

Method: 提出嵌套式预测框架：1) 基于谱聚类构建语义一致区域，理论+实验证明可滤除系统噪声并保留趋势；2) 渐进式粗到细预测器，将宏观未来表征融入微观推理过程；3) 利用趋势预测提前预判周期性偏移等动态异常。

Result: 在多个高维数据集上的大量实验表明，该方法一致优于现有最先进基线，验证了未来宏观引导的嵌套预测的有效性。

Conclusion: 通过宏观区域趋势自上而下引导微观预测的嵌套框架，能够有效应对噪声和非平稳条件下的时空预测挑战，为动态异常预判提供了新思路。

Abstract: Spatiotemporal forecasting is critical for real-world applications like traffic management, yet capturing reliable interactions remains challenging under noisy and non-stationary conditions. Existing methods primarily rely on historical spatial priors, often failing to account for evolving temporal correlations and suffering from systematic errors. In this work, we propose a nested forecasting framework that couples future macro-level regional trends with micro-level historical observations, enabling top-down guidance from abstract future representations for fine-grained forecasting. Specifically, we employ a spectral clustering-based approach to construct semantically coherent regions, providing both theoretical and empirical evidence that this representation effectively filters systematic noise while preserving essential trends. Building on this, we develop a progressive coarse-to-fine predictor to integrate these representative features into the inference process. This enables the model to leverage trend predictions to anticipate dynamic anomalies, such as periodic offsets, in advance. Furthermore, extensive experiments on multiple high-dimensional datasets demonstrate that our method consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, validating the effectiveness of future macro-guided nested forecasting.

### [35] [Identifiable Token Correspondence for World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16457)

Method: 将下一帧重构为结构化概率推断问题，引入潜在令牌对应变量；每个下一帧令牌的来源被建模为两种方式之一：从前一帧复制已有令牌，或生成全新令牌，从而在架构层面强制保持跨帧的对应一致性。

Conclusion: 显式建模令牌间的跨时间对应关系能有效提升世界模型在长程推演中的时间一致性，该方法在多个基准上验证了其有效性，代码已开源。

Abstract: Transformer-based world models have shown strong performance in visual reinforcement learning, but often suffer from temporal inconsistency in long-horizon rollouts, including object duplication, disappearance, and transmutation. A key reason is that most existing approaches treat next-frame prediction purely as a token generation problem, without explicitly modeling correspondence between tokens across time. We formulate next-frame prediction as a structured probabilistic inference problem with latent token correspondence variables, deriving a model in which each next-frame token is explained either by copying a token from the previous frame or by generating a new token. Our experiments show state-of-the-art performance on 4 challenging benchmarks. The proposed method achieves a return of 72.5% and a score of 35.6% on the Craftax-classic benchmark, significantly surpassing the previous best of 67.4% and 27.9%. We release our source code on https://github.com/snu-mllab/Identifiable-Token-Correspondence.

<details>

Method: 提出Creator-Appraiser对偶框架：Creator生成候选样本，Appraiser通过少量内循环学习步骤快速适应该样本，Appraiser的改进程度作为Creator优化目标的奖励信号。使用冻结的扩散模型作为Creator（无额外语言条件），MNIST自编码器或带低秩适配器的CLIP作为Appraiser，通过元学习梯度进行优化。

Conclusion: 创造力可形式化为生成对快速自适应观察者而言具有学习价值的刺激，Creator-Appraiser框架为此提供了一种可行的计算实现。

Abstract: What does it mean to create a new concept, rather than retrieve a familiar one? Repeatedly sampling a generative model at the same prompt produces variations with similar styles and typical content. We propose that creativity is the production of stimuli that are unfamiliar to an adaptive observer at first sight, but quickly learnable from a few exposures. We formalize this as a Creator-Appraiser pair: a Creator generates a candidate, an Appraiser adapts to it for a few inner-loop learning steps, and the Appraiser's improvement becomes the reward the Creator optimizes through. We instantiate the framework with diffusion as the Creator, an autoencoder Appraiser on MNIST, and a CLIP Appraiser with a low-rank adapter for natural images. The diffusion model remains frozen with no additional language conditioning; the meta-learning gradient is enough to produce both stylistic variations and concept compositions that the base model does not generate on its own.

### [37] [Global Convergence of Sampling-Based Nonconvex Optimization through Diffusion-Style Smoothing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16520)
*Zeji Yi,Chaoyi Pan,Guanya Shi,Guannan Qu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过平滑视角对采样优化（SBO）进行非渐近收敛分析，揭示了平滑化带来的覆盖-最优性权衡，并提出了可证明全局收敛的退火SBO算法DIDA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 采样优化方法（如交叉熵方法、进化算法）在无梯度非凸问题中表现优异，但其收敛性理论尚不清晰。本文旨在建立SBO的非渐近收敛分析框架。

Method: 将SBO重新解释为对平滑目标函数的梯度下降（类似扩散模型中的噪声条件得分上升），进行平滑后目标函数的景观分析，提出退火SBO算法DIDA（Diffusion-Inspired Dual-Annealing）。

Result: 揭示了覆盖-最优性权衡：平滑使景观更良性（扩大全局最优附近的局部凸区域），但引入最优性差距。建立了SBO收敛到全局最优邻域的非渐近保证，DIDA可证明收敛到全局最优。

Conclusion: 数值实验验证了景观分析结果，DIDA相比其他无梯度优化方法表现优越。研究结果对扩散模型具有理论启示意义。

Abstract: Sampling-based optimization (SBO), like cross-entropy method and evolutionary algorithms, has achieved many successes in solving non-convex problems without gradients, yet its convergence is poorly understood. In this paper, we establish a non-asymptotic convergence analysis for SBO through the lens of smoothing. Specifically, we recast SBO as gradient descent on a smoothed objective, mirroring noise-conditioned score ascent in diffusion models. Our first contribution is a landscape analysis of the smoothed objective, demonstrating how smoothing helps escape local minima and uncovering a fundamental coverage-optimality trade-off: smoothing renders the landscape more benign by enlarging the locally convex region around the global minimizer, but at the cost of introducing an optimality gap. Building on this insight, we establish non-asymptotic convergence guarantees for SBO algorithms to a neighborhood of the global minimizer. Furthermore, we propose an annealed SBO algorithm, Diffusion-Inspired Dual-Annealing (DIDA), which is provably convergent to the global optimum. We conduct extensive numerical experiments to verify our landscape results and also demonstrate the compelling performance of DIDA compared to other gradient-free optimization methods. Lastly, we discuss implications of our results for diffusion models.

</details>


### [38] [Hypergraph Pattern Machine: Compositional Tokenization for Higher-Order Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16527)
*Kyrie Zhao,Zehong Wang,Tianyi Ma,Fang Wu,Xiangru Tang,Pietro Lio,Sheng Wang,Yanfang Ye*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出超图模式机（HGPM），通过将超图学习范式从消息传递转变为子集组合模式学习，解决了现有方法无法建模高阶交互组合性的问题，在十个基准上达到SOTA，并能区分现有方法无法识别的特征相同但作用相反的药物组合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有超图学习方法仅通过消息传递在观测超边上传播信息，未建模交互组合性（compositionality），即高阶关系是组合性、涌现性还是抑制性的。这一缺陷导致危险药物组合可能被误分类，例如无法区分特征相同但一个药物添加会抑制副作用、另一个不会的情况。

Method: HGPM将子集组合性模式学习作为核心：1）对组合性子集进行token化；2）组织成包含DAG（inclusion DAG）；3）训练一个包含感知的Transformer，在掩码重建目标下学习子集间的包含关系模式。

Result: 在十个超图基准上匹配或超过现有最先进方法；在真实不良事件预测案例中，HGPM能正确识别特征相同的候选药物中哪一个添加后会抑制副作用，这是现有方法无法做到的区分。

Conclusion: HGPM通过显式建模子集组合模式，为超图学习提供了超越消息传递的新范式，在需要组合性推理的高阶关系预测任务（如联合用药安全）中具有关键优势。

Abstract: Hypergraphs model higher-order relations that drive real-world decisions, from drug prescriptions to recommendations. A central structural signal in such data, beyond what pairwise relations can express, is interaction compositionality: whether a higher-order relation is compositional, emergent, or inhibitory with respect to its observed or unobserved sets. In polypharmacy, the regime decides whether a drug should be dropped, kept, or excluded: a compositional drug triple can be safely simplified, an emergent triple requires all drugs jointly, and an inhibitory triple flags a drug that disrupts an existing interaction. However, existing hypergraph learning methods, which merely propagate messages over observed hyperedges, leave this compositional signal unmodeled, allowing dangerous drug combinations to slip through and be misclassified. To this end, we propose the Hypergraph Pattern Machine (HGPM), shifting the paradigm from message passing to learning the compositional pattern of subsets. It tokenizes compositional subsets, organizes them in an inclusion DAG, and trains an inclusion-aware Transformer under masked reconstruction. On ten hypergraph benchmarks, HGPM matches or exceeds state-of-the-art methods. Notably, in a real adverse-event prediction case, HGPM correctly identifies the drug addition that inhibits the side effect among feature-identical candidates, a discrimination existing methods cannot make. The code and data are in https://github.com/KryieZhao/HGPM.git.

</details>

### [40] [Boundedly Rational Meta-Learning in Sequential Consumer Choice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16532)
*Mehrzad Khosravi,Max Kleiman-Weiner,Hema Yoganarasimhan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过层次化实验室任务研究消费者在重复选择中的跨情境知识迁移（元学习），发现参与者能跨航线学习，但采用的是有限理性的元动态规划策略（BRMDP(1)），即用粗粒度的先验不确定性表征进行近似迁移，而非完全贝叶斯整合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型假设学习在进入新情境时重新开始，但现实中消费者会将先前的品牌经验迁移到后续相关决策中。本文旨在系统研究这种跨情境知识迁移（元学习）在序贯选择中的作用机制。

Method: 设计层次化实验室任务：参与者多次在不同航线中选择航空公司，观察带有噪声的二元结果。提出有限理性元动态规划策略BRMDP(D)，用有限数量的超后验样本来近似完全整合。通过逐试次似然比较评估不同模型的拟合度。

Result: 参与者在航线内和跨航线均表现出学习改进；有限理性元学习模型（特别是BRMDP(1)）比无迁移和完全贝叶斯迁移模型更好地拟合了参与者行为。

Conclusion: 消费者能跨情境迁移品牌层面的规律，但仅通过粗粒度的先验不确定性表征进行近似迁移。消费者学习模型应考虑近似跨情境迁移，纯粹的无迁移或完全整合模型可能导致误导性反事实推断。

Abstract: Many consumer decisions are repeated choices under uncertainty. Standard models capture these decisions using Bayesian learning and dynamic programming: consumers update beliefs from feedback and use those beliefs to guide future choices. In many markets, however, learning does not restart when consumers enter a new context: prior experience with a brand, product, or provider can shape beliefs in later, related decisions. We study this cross-context knowledge transfer, or meta-learning, in sequential choice. We design a hierarchical laboratory task in which participants repeatedly choose among airlines across routes and observe noisy binary outcomes. Reduced-form evidence shows that participants improve not only within routes, but also across routes: they choose better airlines earlier in later routes and reduce pseudo-regret. To identify the mechanism behind this transfer, we compare human choices to a no-transfer benchmark and a fully integrated Bayesian meta-learning benchmark. In particular, we introduce a class of boundedly rational meta dynamic programming policies, BRMDP(D), that approximate full integration using a limited number of hyper-posterior draws, denoted by D. Trial-by-trial likelihood comparisons show that low-D boundedly rational meta-learning, especially BRMDP(1), fits participant behavior better than both no transfer and fully integrated Bayesian transfer. Consumers, therefore, transfer brand-level regularities across contexts, but through coarse representations of prior uncertainty. The findings imply that models of consumer learning should allow for approximate cross-context transfer, and that managerial counterfactuals based on either no-transfer or fully integrated learning can be misleading.

To address this gap, this paper investigates goal-oriented semantic communications for physical AI systems with closed-loop sensing-communication-inference-control. Abstract: Accurate emulation of multi-scale physical systems governed by PDEs demands models that remain stable over long autoregressive rollouts while preserving fine-scale structures. We propose Wavelet Flow Matching (WFM), a novel generative emulator that overcomes current trade-offs between cost and skill by performing optimal-transport directly in the multi-scale wavelet space. Rather than learning a latent compression, WFM leverages the hierarchical structure of a U-Net to jointly predict transport velocities of a prescribed wavelet representation. On three challenging systems of chaotic fluid dynamics, WFM achieves superior long-horizon stability, accuracy and spectral coherence compared to state-of-the-art models. Abstract: Masked language modeling (MLM) is the standard objective for training protein language models, typically implemented by randomly masking individual residues at a fixed rate (e.g., 15%). This practice implicitly assumes that all sequence positions contribute equally to representation learning. By conditioning the masking distribution on residue contacts, Bucket Masking shifts the learning objective toward modeling long-range interactions that are critical for protein function. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对上下文学习机制的认知仍不完善，缺乏对少样本提示如何塑造模型函数向量的因果解释。

Method: 通过线性分解将n-shot函数向量表示为示例级子函数向量的线性组合；分析注意力机制中示例表征的上下文依赖性；通过因果分解分离Query-Key路由与Value更新在函数向量形成中的作用。

Result: n-shot函数向量可被示例级子函数向量线性逼近；模型根据上下文自适应地重加权示例贡献，注意力更倾向于信息量高、歧义低的示例；Query-Key对齐在歧义情境下对函数向量质量贡献最一致，Value介导的效果则更具异质性。

Conclusion: 将加性叠加与上下文相关的注意力重加权统一到一个可验证的因果机制中，为理解少样本提示如何实现任务执行提供了系统性的解释。

Abstract: In-context learning (ICL) excels at new tasks from minimal examples, yet we still lack a mechanistic explanation of how few-shot prompts shape a model's function vector (FV)--a causal activation direction that drives task behavior on the ICL query. Across tasks and models, an $n$-shot FV is well-approximated by a linear combination of example-level sub-FVs, suggesting additive and composable contributions from individual demonstrations. Beyond additivity, we show that models contextualize individual examples' representations based on prior examples to adaptively reweight which demonstrations dominate the FV: attention shifts toward examples that are more informative and less ambiguous under the context. Finally, a causal decomposition separates Query-Key routing from Value updates, finding that contextualization's most consistent contributions to FV quality arise from Query-Key alignment--particularly in ambiguous settings--while Value-mediated effects are more heterogeneous. Together, these results unify additive superposition with context-dependent attention reweighting into a mechanistic, testable account of how few-shot prompts implement tasks.

### [46] [Where Pretraining writes and Alignment reads: the asymmetry of Transformer weight space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16600)
*Valeria Ruscio,Eli-Shaoul Khedouri,Keiran Thompson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过相对子空间分数探针，揭示了交叉熵预训练和偏好对齐在Transformer权重空间中留下不同的几何痕迹：读路径（W_Q, W_K）的权重更新集中在注意力输入激活的主方向上，而写路径（W_O, W_2）的更新相对于预测子空间保持近各向同性。这种不对称性源于各向异性梯度累积——读路径的输入激活协方差呈尖峰结构导致目标无关的集中，写路径的上游梯度各向异性则依赖于损失函数。交叉熵提供尖锐的逐样本信号产生写路径预测几何，而对齐目标几乎不增加额外写侧集中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解交叉熵预训练和偏好对齐这两种不同训练范式在Transformer权重空间中留下的几何痕迹差异，以及这种不对称性背后的机制。

Method: 提出相对子空间分数探针，跟踪权重增量与残差流激活子空间及由解嵌入定义的预测子空间的对齐程度；通过各向异性梯度累积的理论分析，对比读路径（W_Q, W_K）和写路径（W_O, W_2）的更新结构差异。

Result: 读路径权重更新集中在注意力输入激活的主方向上，写路径更新相对于预测子空间保持近各向同性；交叉熵预训练在写路径产生预测几何结构，而对齐目标几乎不增加额外写侧集中。

Conclusion: 权重空间几何的不对称性由各向异性梯度累积解释，并通过检查点轨迹、对比目标控制和秩1干预实验提供了因果证据。

Abstract: Cross-entropy pretraining and preference alignment update the same transformer weights, but leave geometrically distinct traces. We characterise this asymmetry with a relative-subspace-fraction probe that tracks how weight deltas align with residual-stream activation subspaces and with the prediction subspace defined by the unembedding. Alignment deltas concentrate in the read pathway ($W_Q$, $W_K$), along principal directions of attention-input activations, while remaining near-isotropic in the write pathway ($W_O$, $W_2$) relative to the prediction subspace. We explain this pattern through anisotropic gradient accumulation: updates to a matrix $W$ are sums of outer products $δ_t a_t^\top$, and inherit directional structure from whichever side has concentrated covariance. For read-pathway matrices, this side is the input activation $a_t$, whose covariance is spiked in trained transformers and therefore produces objective-agnostic concentration. For write-pathway matrices, the relevant side is the upstream gradient $δ_t$, whose anisotropy depends on the loss. Cross-entropy supplies the canonical sharp per-sample signal, inducing write-pathway prediction geometry during pretraining; alignment objectives typically add little further write-side concentration. We support this explanation with a within-checkpoint trajectory, a graded contrastive-objective control, and a closed-form rank-1 intervention with matched direction controls, providing causal evidence for the proposed weight-space geometry.

Abstract: Matryoshka Representation Learning (MRL) is a widely adopted approach for training text encoders so they provide useful text representations at various sizes, available by simply truncating the resulting vectors at sizes pre-determined at training time. Recent works have shown that randomly truncating text embeddings has minimal impact in downstream performance unless vectors are reduced in size by at least 70%, suggesting that embeddings are already robust to truncation without the use of MRL. However, no prior work has compared random truncation to MRL, so it is unclear how the two methods compare as effective embedding reduction methods. In this paper, we study this by applying the same truncation used by MRL to models trained with and without MRL. Our results across several models and downstream tasks show that, unless heavily truncating embeddings (i.e. reducing their size by at least 80%), truncated embeddings of non-MRL models are competitive with, and often outperform models trained with MRL. This suggests that truncation robustness may not necessarily come from MRL, and that the choice of spending the additional training cost of MRL depends on whether heavy truncation is desired.

We focus on the fundamental question of learning these preferences.
  Many applications of this problem make specific modeling assumptions on evaluator preferences that may be substantially violated in the real world. We make the minimal assumption that the preference function is coordinate-wise non-decreasing, which is reasonable in a large number of evaluation settings. We theoretically characterize the severity of model mismatch for many common assumptions and show that it can lead to significant issues for learning evaluator preferences and other important downstream tasks. We then present an algorithm for learning evaluators' preferences that is robust to model mismatch. Evaluations of our algorithm with synthetic simulations and real-world data confirm its ability to learn preferences robustly and illustrate key aspects of LLM and human preferences.

### [49] [MLReplicate: Benchmarking Autonomous Research Systems for Machine Learning Reproducibility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16616)
*Sasi Kiran Gaddipati,Diyana Muhammed,Farhana Keya,Gollam Rabby,Sören Auer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MLReplicate是一个评估自主科研系统在机器学习可重复性方面能力的端到端基准测试。通过对ICML 2025杰出论文的重现实验，评估了6个前沿系统，发现所有系统都存在方法缺陷、幻觉实验结果和可重复性失败，且59%被自动评审接受的论文包含伪造或无法支持的声明。研究表明工作流设计比计算规模更重要，揭示了当前自主科研系统与真正科学严谨性之间的显著差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主科研系统生成完整科学手稿的能力快速进步，但缺乏稳健且现实的评估框架来准确衡量这些系统的实际科研能力。

Method: 基于ICML 2025杰出论文构建标准化输入规范，评估6个前沿自主科研系统（AI SCIENTIST-V1/V2, AGENT LABORATORY, CYCLERESEARCHER, AI RESEARCHER, TINY SCIENTIST），共生成45份手稿（3份失败）。采用双协议评估：自动会议式评审+结构化专家人工评审，同时跟踪计算成本、运行时间和人工干预量。

Result: 自动评审接受了37份有效提交中的10份，另有8份因页数不足被直接拒稿。人工评审发现所有系统均存在方法缺陷、幻觉实验和可重复性失败，59%被自动评审接受的论文含有伪造或无法支持的声明。最廉价的系统在人工评审中表现优于最昂贵的系统（输入token相差38倍），表明工作流设计比计算规模更重要。

Conclusion: 当前自主科研系统与真正科学严谨性之间存在显著差距，MLReplicate为系统化推进可信赖的AI驱动科学发现提供了实用且可扩展的评估框架。

Abstract: Autonomous research systems capable of generating complete scientific manuscripts have advanced rapidly, yet robust and realistic evaluation frameworks have failed to keep pace. To bridge this gap, we introduce MLReplicate, an end-to-end benchmark evaluating autonomous research systems on machine learning reproducibility. The benchmark was constructed from ICML 2025 outstanding papers reformulated into standardized input specifications and evaluated across 6 state-of-the-art research systems: AI SCIENTIST-V1, AI SCIENTIST-V2, AGENT LABORATORY, CYCLERESEARCHER, AI RESEARCHER, and TINY SCIENTIST, yielding 45 generated manuscripts, with 3 failed experiments. Outputs are assessed using a dual-protocol approach that combines automated conference-style review and structured expert human evaluation, while tracking computational cost, runtime, and the amount of required human intervention. The automated conference-style review accepted 10 out of 37 valid submissions. An additional 8 submissions were desk-rejected before review for failing to meet the minimum page threshold. In contrast to automated reviews, human reviewers consistently identified methodological flaws, hallucinated experimental results, and reproducibility failures across all systems, and 59% of accepted automated reviews contained fabricated or unsupported claims. We further find that neither token budget nor computational cost predicts output quality: the cheapest system outperforms the most resource-intensive system in human evaluation, despite a 38-fold difference in input tokens. We thus demonstrate that autonomous research workflow design matters more than the scale of compute. MLReplicate exposes a substantial gap between current autonomous research systems and genuine scientific rigor, and establishes a practical, extensible evaluation framework for systematic progress toward trustworthy AI-driven scientific discovery.

</details>


### [50] [SCOUT: Cyclic Causal Discovery Under Soft Interventions with Unknown Targets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16620)
*Alpar Turkoglu,Muralikrishnna G. Sethuraman,Faramarz Fekri*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SCOUT是一个能从软干预数据中学习非线性循环因果关系并恢复未知干预目标的新型因果发现框架，使用归一化流架构，在合成和真实数据上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有因果发现算法大多假设系统无环、噪声高斯、干预目标已知，但这些假设在现实系统中常被违反。现有方法要么假设线性模型，要么局限于有限的干预设置，因此需要一种能处理非线性循环因果关系且干预目标未知的方法。

Method: 提出SCOUT框架，通过最大化数据对数似然来恢复图结构，采用两种归一化流架构：收缩残差流(contractive residual flows)和神经样条流(neural spline flows)来建模非线性循环因果关系。

Result: 在合成数据和真实数据上的实验表明，SCOUT在多种干预和噪声设置下，在因果图恢复和未知目标恢复方面均优于现有最先进方法。

Conclusion: SCOUT成功解决了现有方法在非线性循环因果发现及未知干预目标场景下的局限性，证明了归一化流在该任务中的有效性。

Abstract: Learning causal relationships between variables from data is a fundamental research area with many applications across disciplines. Most existing causal discovery algorithms rely on the assumptions that (i) the underlying system is acyclic, (ii) the exogenous noise variables are Gaussian, and (iii) the intervention targets for the data-generating experiments are known. While these assumptions simplify the analysis, they are violated in real-life systems. Most existing methods that address these issues either assume the underlying model is linear or are constrained to operate in limited interventional settings. To that end, we propose SCOUT, a novel causal discovery framework for learning nonlinear cyclic causal relationships from soft interventional data with unknown targets. Our approach maximizes the data log-likelihood to recover the graph structure, using two normalizing-flow architectures: contractive residual flows and neural spline flows. Through experiments on synthetic and real-world data, we show that SCOUT outperforms state-of-the-art methods in both causal graph recovery and unknown target recovery across various interventional and noise settings.

### [51] [Does Weight Decay Enhance Training Stability?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16622)
*Marius Saether,Amir Kolic,Tomaso Poggio,Pierfrancesco Beneventano*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了权重衰减（weight decay）对深度学习训练动态稳定性的影响机制，发现权重衰减能有效减缓"渐进锐化"现象，并在CNN和MLP中表现出不同的架构依赖相变行为，通过参数向量与锐度梯度的全局对齐解释了该相变机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究权重衰减是否以及如何稳定训练动态，因为现代深度学习中权重衰减常被认为具有"稳定"训练的作用，但这一机制尚未被充分理解。

Method: 在Edge of Stability (EoS)框架下分析权重衰减对参数空间动态和损失锐度的影响，通过数学建模和实验观察CNN与MLP中的相变现象，并利用NTK分析函数空间稳定性。

Result: 权重衰减能稳健地减缓渐进锐化；在CNN中抑制EoS处的振荡，在MLP中引发相变使锐度稳定在低于理论阈值2/η的水平；参数向量与锐度梯度的全局对齐是相变的机制驱动因素。

Conclusion: 权重衰减通过全局对齐机制影响训练稳定性，且基于凸/二次启发式的曲率阈值在正则化下不可靠，这为理解深度学习中的训练动态提供了新视角。

Abstract: In modern deep learning, weight decay is often credited with "stabilizing" training dynamics, diverging from its classical role as a static regularization penalty. We investigate a fundamental question: *does weight decay stabilize training dynamics, and if so, through which mechanism?* Indeed, training stability is understood through different but related notions in the literature. We consider how weight decay affects the parameter-space dynamics and loss sharpness by analyzing its effects at the \emph{Edge of Stability} (EoS). We show that weight decay robustly slows *progressive sharpening}. Furthermore, we uncover a striking architecture-dependent phase transition. In CNNs, weight decay dampens the oscillations at the EoS, while in MLPs, increasing weight decay causes a phase transition in which the sharpness stabilizes at a threshold significantly below the theoretical $\frac{2}η$ boundary. We develop a mathematical framework that accurately models these phenomena and identify the global alignment of the parameter vector and the sharpness gradient as the mechanistic driver of the phase transition. Importantly, we show that these phenomena translate into stability in terms of search in function-space (NTK). Last, this shows that curvature thresholds obtained from convex/quadratic heuristics may not be reliable stability diagnostics under regularization.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Cube-and-Conquer（C&C）在解决挑战性SAT问题中非常有效，但此前没有工作证明基于Transformer的模型能够学习有效的立方分割启发式。
