Conclusion: Transformer可以被训练以在传统由符号方法主导的领域中做出有效的立方分割决策。

Abstract: Despite the effectiveness of Cube-and-Conquer (C&C) for solving challenging Boolean Satisfiability (SAT) problems, no prior work has shown that transformer-based models can learn effective cubing heuristics. We introduce a neuro-symbolic post-training framework for this task. We design an MCTS-based data curation pipeline that uses symbolic heuristics to explore splitting decisions over SAT competition formulas, producing preference data grounded in solver statistics and augmented with reasoning traces from a teacher model. Our two-stage post-training, supervised fine-tuning (SFT) followed by direct preference optimization (DPO), enables a 4B-parameter model to achieve a pass@5 score of 53 on 100 SAT competition benchmarks, surpassing frontier LLMs such as Claude-Sonnet-4 (50) and matching the best symbolic heuristic (53). Ablations show that SFT alone improves pass@5 from 46 to 51, with DPO adding 2 additional benchmarks; an entropy/agreement ablation on realized first-cube decisions further shows that SFT, not DPO, accounts for the root-level decision diversity that produces complementary per-run coverage over deterministic symbolic methods. This demonstrates that transformers can be trained to make effective cubing decisions in a domain traditionally dominated by symbolic methods.

Conclusion: MedMIX是一个实用的多模态框架，统一了模态内专家协作、样本特异性跨模态融合和高效的大-小模型协作，同时对不完整模态保持鲁棒性。

Abstract: Multimodal clinical prediction faces three challenges: multiple foundation models (FMs) with complementary strengths per modality, pervasive missing modalities at training and test time, and sample-specific variation in modality contributions. We introduce MedMIX, a multimodal framework that combines intra-modality expert fusion, learned inter-modality fusion, and training-only large--small model collaboration for robust medical prediction under incomplete modalities. Within each modality, MedMIX aggregates complementary embeddings from multiple small expert models; across modalities, it performs learned fusion over available modalities; and during training, it leverages large teacher models to improve deployed representations without additional inference cost. Across three heterogeneous benchmarks (OpenI, MIMIC-IV-MM, and MMIST-ccRCC), MedMIX achieves consistently strong performance while remaining robust under controlled missing-modality perturbations, and further demonstrates sustained robustness under cross-cohort shift on MIMIC-III. These results highlight MedMIX as a practical framework that unifies within-modality expert collaboration, sample-specific cross-modality fusion, and efficient large--small model collaboration while remaining robust to incomplete modalities.

We show that there is. We define parity-conditioned retrieval task and show that under constant-precision assumption, a Qwen-style hybrid of Gated DeltaNet and Gated Attention solves this task with a constant scratchpad, or equivalently $O(1)$ chain-of-thought steps. Abstract: Continental-scale knowledge of subsurface temperature is limited by the cost and sparsity of borehole measurements, but such information is essential for geothermal resource assessment and for understanding heat transport in the shallow crust. Here we introduce In-Context Earth, a transformer-based model that uses sparse local borehole observations as geological context to predict continuous temperature-at-depth fields with calibrated uncertainty. Interpretability analyses show that the model learns internal representations of subsurface properties it never observes during training, including seismic velocities, geochemistry, and crustal structure, and uses these representations in physically consistent ways. More broadly, this work shows that in-context learning can use sparse borehole observations for continental-scale subsurface characterization, without requiring dense measurements or region-specific retraining.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用MoE层的张量结构，在专家级别忠实建模编辑目标；应用Woodbury矩阵恒等式避免完整专家权重矩阵的构造和求逆；将更新简化为固定低秩矩阵的求逆，无需额外反向传播。

This mismatch leaves a growing class of production models without principled editing tools. We propose a MEMIT-like framework for knowledge editing in MoE-based LLMs. Our method exploits the tensor structure of MoE layers to formulate the editing objective faithfully at the per expert level, and applies the Woodbury matrix identity to avoid materializing or inverting the full stacked matrix of expert weights. The resulting update reduces to inversions of fixed low-rank matrices and requires no additional backward passes. Empirically, our approach matches the editing quality of strong baselines on the main KE metrics while accelerating the editing procedure by up to 6x, owing to the batched MEMIT-style formulation and the low-dimensional inversions enabled by the Woodbury identity. These results show that closed-form, parameter-modifying KE can be extended efficiently beyond dense layers, opening a path toward scalable knowledge editing in modern sparse LLM architectures.

We argue that this is not an analogy. It is the same operational problem actuarial science has been tooled for decades to address, restated with new dependent variables (tokens, bandwidth bytes, function-invocations, gym check-ins) in place of medical claims. This paper proposes a modeling framework for capped-usage SaaS pricing built from frequency-severity decomposition, premium calculation principles, and Monte Carlo reserve adequacy. *Siqi Zeng,Christopher Jung,Rui Li,Zhe Kang,Ming Li,Nima Noorshams,Zhigang Wang,Fuchun Peng,Han Zhao,Xue Feng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了LLM后训练阶段数据集的子集选择与价值评估问题，提出了一种基于梯度空间核均值匹配（KMM）的可扩展凸优化方法，在考虑目标任务对齐性和数据集间冗余性的同时，在有限预算下最大化下游任务性能。实验表明该方法优于现有基线，且计算开销低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在后训练阶段，开发者面临计算、标注和许可成本约束，无法使用所有辅助数据集；数据集市场（marketplaces）的出现进一步引入了预算和谈判机制。现有基于梯度对齐的评分方法仅考虑单个数据集与目标的相关性，忽略了数据集之间的冗余，导致次优选择。因此，需要一种能在预算约束下联合考虑对齐性与冗余性的数据集级子集选择与加权方法。

Method: 提出基于梯度空间核均值匹配（Kernel Mean Matching, KMM）的凸数据集级估值方法。首先计算每个辅助数据集与目标任务在梯度空间中的分布，然后通过KMM在约束预算下联合优化数据集的权重，同时兼顾与目标任务的对齐性和数据之间的冗余性。该方法可扩展（scalable）且为凸优化问题，便于求解。

Result: 在多种后训练设置（如监督微调、RLHF等）和任务上，该方法一致优于现有的数据集估值基线（如梯度对齐评分等），在同等预算下实现了更强的下游任务性能，且计算开销低。

Conclusion: 数据集估值可以作为市场约束下LLM后训练数据选择的有效决策工具。所提方法既考虑了目标对齐性又考虑了冗余性，在实用性和性能之间取得了良好平衡。

Abstract: Improving LLM performance on downstream tasks sometimes requires leveraging auxiliary datasets during post-training. In practice, however, developers face constraints on compute, labeling, and licensing costs that preclude using all available data, necessitating principled dataset-level selection. These constraints are increasingly shaped by dataset marketplaces, where data acquisition is governed by budgets and negotiation. We study dataset valuation as a subset selection problem during LLM post-training. Our goal is to identify and weight auxiliary datasets so as to maximize target task performance given constrained budgets. We first show that commonly used gradient alignment scores provide a reasonable yet incomplete valuation signal, as they ignore redundancy among datasets. To address this, we propose a scalable convex dataset-level valuation method based on kernel mean matching (KMM) in gradient space, which jointly accounts for alignment with the target task and redundancy across auxiliary datasets. Through extensive experiments across diverse post-training settings and tasks, we show that our approach consistently outperforms existing valuation baselines, achieving stronger performance with low computational overhead. Our results position dataset valuation as a practical decision tool for post-training data selection in market-constrained large language model settings. The code is available at https://github.com/uiuctml/convex_data_valuation.

</details>


### [59] [EmoMind: Decoding Affective Captions from Human Brain fMRI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16739)
*Bilal A. Mohammed,Lin Gu,Ruogo Fang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EmoMind是首个直接从fMRI信号解码情感字幕的端到端管线，通过连续34维情感向量改写语义场景描述，在内容保留与情感表达间实现可控插值，在三轴验证框架（主体特异性、结构几何、因果控制）上显著优于标签提示的GPT-4基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有脑到文本系统仅恢复语义内容而丢弃情感信息；语言模型虽能生成情感文本但依赖离散类别标签，无法捕捉个体间丰富的情感变异。因此需要一种能从脑信号中解码连续情感表示并用于个性化情感字幕生成的方法。

Method: EmoMind包含两阶段：1) 从fMRI解码的视觉特征中检索语义中立的场景描述；2) 利用同一fMRI记录的连续34维情感向量改写该描述。采用无分类器引导训练重写器，通过身份保持空分支实现语义保真度与情感表现力之间的平滑插值。评估采用三轴验证框架（主体特异性、结构几何、因果控制）并增加合成脑替代测试，以标签提示的GPT-4作为离散基线。

Result: 在两个独立情感fMRI数据集上，EmoMind在所有三个验证轴上显著优于标签提示的GPT-4，尤其在需要个体特异性情感结构的指标上增益最大。

Conclusion: 连续脑解码情感可作为个性化情感字幕生成的可行控制信号，为研究个体情感脑组织开辟新方向。

Abstract: Decoding visual experience from brain activity has advanced substantially, but cur- rent brain-to-text systems largely recover semantic content while discarding affect. Additionally, language models can generate emotional text when prompted with categorical labels, but such labels collapse rich inter-subject variability into coarse discrete bins. We present EmoMind, the first end-to-end pipeline for decoding affective captions directly from fMRI signals. EmoMind first retrieves a semanti- cally grounded neutral scene description from brain-decoded visual features, then rewrites it using a continuous 34-dimensional emotion vector decoded from the same fMRI recording. To control the balance between content preservation and affective expression, we train the rewriter with classifier-free guidance against an identity-preserving null branch, enabling smooth interpolation between semantic fidelity and affective expressivity. We evaluate affective caption generation with a three-axis validation framework spanning subject-specificity, structural geometry, and causal control. We further augment this framework with a synthetic-brain substitution test that probes robustness to the measurement apparatus, and we benchmark each axis against GPT-4 prompted with brain-decoded top-5 emotion labels as a strong discrete baseline. Across two independent emotion fMRI datasets, EmoMind significantly outperforms label-prompted GPT-4 on all three axes, with the largest gains on metrics that require person-specific affective structure rather than population-level emotion aggregation. These results establish continuous brain-decoded affect as a viable control signal for individualized affective cap- tion generation and open new directions for studying individual affective brain organisation.

### [60] [Propagation of Chaos in Contextual Flow Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16747)
*Shi Chen,Zhengjiang Lin,Kaizhao Liu,Philippe Rigollet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了上下文流映射（CFMs）的抽象框架，用于在大上下文场景下定量统计理解Transformer。通过将有限上下文模型近似为理想化的无限上下文系统，利用McKean-Vlasov动力学和混沌传播机制，建立了有限与无限上下文CFM之间沿深度的前向偏差界和沿在线梯度下降迭代的后向偏差界，分别达到最优Wasserstein速率$n^{-1/d}$和参数速率$n^{-1/2}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大上下文场景下，对Transformer进行定量统计理论分析，理解上下文长度作为统计资源的作用机制。

Method: 提出了上下文流映射（CFMs）抽象框架，将有限上下文模型近似为无限上下文系统（用总体分布替代上下文测度），利用McKean-Vlasov动力学结构和混沌传播理论，推导出前向与后向偏差界，并提出了新的欧拉伴随公式来分析损失梯度。

Result: 前向偏差界达到最优Wasserstein速率$n^{-1/d}$（适用于一般CFM），后向偏差界达到参数速率$n^{-1/2}$（适用于包含Transformer的受限CFM类）。

Conclusion: 建立了Transformer在大上下文场景下的统计学习理论，揭示了上下文长度$n$作为统计资源的核心作用，所提出的前向-伴随系统稳定性估计方法具有独立的研究价值。

Abstract: We develop a quantitative statistical theory of transformers in the large-context regime by adopting the abstraction of contextual flow maps (CFMs): dynamical systems that evolve a distinguished token in the presence of a contextual measure across a stack of attention blocks. Within this framework, the finite-context model approximates an idealized infinite-context system in which the contextual measure is replaced by its underlying population, so that the context length $n$ becomes a statistical resource. Exploiting the McKean--Vlasov structure of the dynamics and the classical machinery of propagation of chaos, we establish a forward bound controlling the deviation between the finite- and infinite-context CFMs uniformly along depth, and a backward bound controlling the deviation between the corresponding training trajectories uniformly across iterations of online gradient descent. Both bounds achieve the optimal Wasserstein rate $n^{-1/d}$ for general CFMs and parametric rate $n^{-1/2}$ for a restricted class of CFMs that includes transformers as a special case. The analysis rests on a new Eulerian adjoint formulation of the loss gradient and stability estimates for the resulting forward--adjoint system, both of which may be of independent interest.

### [61] [Learning Unbiased Permutations via Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16755)
*Yimeng Min,Carla P. Gomes*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PermFlow是一种基于条件流匹配的框架，直接在行和列和为单位矩阵的仿射子空间上操作，通过闭式切空间投影器保持置换约束，使用最近目标耦合区分不同噪声初始化，从而捕获多模态置换分布，避免Sinkhorn方法在歧义下坍缩的问题。在视觉排序和对称线性分配任务中，PermFlow在无歧义输入上实现高精度，在歧义下恢复两种有效置换，而Sinkhorn基线方法结构性失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于熵正则化Sinkhorn的可微置换方法只能产生单一软化解，在存在歧义时会发生坍缩，无法捕获多模态的置换分布。

Method: 提出PermFlow框架：在行和列和为单位矩阵的仿射子空间上直接操作；设计闭式切空间投影器确保轨迹上严格保持置换约束（无需迭代校正）；引入最近目标耦合机制将不同噪声初始化路由到不同的有效置换。

Result: 在混合数字歧义的视觉排序任务和对称线性分配问题上，PermFlow在无歧义输入上达到高精度，在歧义下能恢复两种有效置换，而Sinkhorn基线方法结构性失败。

Conclusion: PermFlow通过流匹配框架有效捕获多模态置换分布，克服了Sinkhorn方法在歧义下坍缩至单一模式的根本局限。

Abstract: Learning permutations is fundamental to sorting, ranking, and matching, but existing differentiable methods based on entropy-regularized Sinkhorn produce a single softened solution and collapse under ambiguity. We present PermFlow, a conditional flow matching framework that operates directly on the affine subspace of matrices with unit row and column sums. A closed-form tangent-space projector preserves these constraints exactly along every trajectory, by construction rather than through iterative correction, and a nearest-target coupling routes distinct noisy initializations toward distinct valid permutations. The result is a model that captures multimodal permutation distributions rather than collapsing them to a single mode. On a visual sorting task with blended-digit ambiguity and a symmetric linear assignment problem, PermFlow achieves high accuracy on unambiguous inputs and recovers both valid permutations under ambiguity, where Sinkhorn-based baselines structurally fail.

### [62] [Distinguishable Deletion: Unifying Knowledge Erasure and Refusal for Large Language Model Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16776)
*Puning Yang,Junchi Yu,Qizhou Wang,Philip Torr,Bo Han,Xiuying Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为Distinguishable Deletion (D²)的范式，通过基于能量的方法在潜在表示层面约束响应分布，而非针对特定token，以实现对LLM中 undesirable 知识的可区分删除，并配套提出了Energy-based Unlearning Alignment (EUA)方法，在训练和推理阶段分别进行能量边界遗忘和能量基拒绝机制，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM安全对齐方法存在两大问题：(1) 基于知识删除(KD)的遗忘方法因压制特定token序列作为完整知识删除的替代，导致有偏删除；(2) 基于可区分拒绝(DR)的遗忘方法因底层知识保持不变，存在有害知识重新出现的风险。两种范式均无法有效解决有害知识的安全处理问题。

Method: 提出D²范式，在潜在表示层面约束响应分布而非特定token来擦除 undesirable 知识，同时将其与保留知识区分开。具体实现为引入能量指数(energy index)来量化知识的存在性以及未学习内容与保留内容之间的分离度，并基于此设计Energy-based Unlearning Alignment (EUA)方法：训练时强制执行能量边界遗忘，推理时应用基于能量的拒绝机制。

Result: 数学和实证分析表明能量指数既准确又高效。大量实验证明EUA显著优于以往方法，验证了D²范式的优越性。

Conclusion: D²范式通过潜在表示层面的能量约束，有效解决了KD的偏删除和DR的重现风险问题，为LLM安全部署提供了一种更优的遗忘对齐方案。

Abstract: Mitigating sensitive and harmful outputs is fundamental to ensuring safe deployment of LLMs. Existing approaches typically follow two paradigms: Knowledge Deletion (KD), which erases undesirable information during training, and Distinguishable Refusal (DR), which steers models away from using sensitive knowledge during inference. Despite rapid progress, KD-based unlearning struggles with biased deletion due to suppressing specific token sequences as a substitute for complete knowledge removal, whereas DR-based unlearning risks the re-emergence of harmful knowledge because the underlying knowledge remains intact. To address these issues, we propose Distinguishable Deletion ($\mathrm{D^2}$), a paradigm that restricts the response distribution in the latent representation rather than specific tokens to erase undesirable knowledge, while distinguishing it from retained knowledge, enabling a refusal mechanism to handle unlearned inputs safely and coherently. To implement $\mathrm{D^2}$, we introduce an energy index that quantifies the presence of knowledge and the separation between unlearned and retained content. Mathematical and empirical analyses show that energy is both accurate and efficient, enabling Energy-based Unlearning Alignment (EUA) to enforce energy-boundary unlearning during training and apply an energy-based refusal mechanism at inference. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EUA significantly outperforms previous methods, indicating the superiority of $\mathrm{D^2}$. Our code is available at https://github.com/Puning97/EUA-for-LLM-Unlearning.

</details>


### [63] [Lever: Speculative LLM Inference on Smartphones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16786)
*Tuowei Wang,Fengzu Li,Yanfan Sun,Wei Gao,Ju Ren*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Lever是一个专为智能手机设计的端到端系统，通过联合优化推测解码的三个阶段（草稿生成、验证、执行），在闪存支持下实现LLM推理加速，相比基线闪存卸载推理平均降低2.93倍延迟，相比传统推测解码降低1.50倍延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在交互式移动应用中需求日益增长，但高质量模型无法完全放入智能手机有限的DRAM中。闪存可存储更大模型，但闪存支持的推理因自回归解码反复调用目标模型而导致I/O开销大、速度慢。现有推测解码方法假设服务器级加速器，未考虑移动端I/O延迟、计算并行度有限及推测执行不规则等问题。

Method: Lever在移动约束下联合优化推测解码三阶段：(1) 草稿阶段：使用I/O和计算感知的增益-成本目标构建token树；(2) 验证阶段：通过早期退出预测修剪低价值分支，减少目标模型计算量；(3) 执行阶段：在移动CPU-NPU硬件上高效映射推测执行，提高硬件利用率。

Result: 相比基线闪存卸载推理，平均降低2.93倍推理延迟；相比传统推测解码，平均降低1.50倍推理延迟，缩小了闪存支持与内存驻留LLM推理之间的延迟差距。

Conclusion: Lever证明了对推测解码进行移动端定制优化可有效缓解闪存推理的延迟瓶颈，使智能手机能搭载更大规模的语言模型。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly needed for interactive mobile applications, but high-quality models exceed the limited DRAM available on smartphones. Flash storage can hold larger models, yet flash-backed inference is slow because autoregressive decoding repeatedly invokes the target model and incurs costly I/O. We observe that speculative decoding is a natural fit for this setting: a small draft model can remain in DRAM, while a larger flash-resident target model verifies multiple candidate tokens per invocation. However, existing methods assume server-class accelerators and fail to account for prolonged I/O latency, limited computation parallelism, and irregular speculation execution.
  We present Lever, an end-to-end system for efficient flash-backed LLM inference on smartphones. Lever jointly optimizes the three stages of speculative decoding under mobile constraints. For drafting, it builds token trees using an I/O- and compute-aware gain-cost objective. For verification, it prunes low-value branches through early-exit prediction to reduce target-model computation. For execution, it maps speculation efficiently across mobile CPU-NPU hardware to improve utilization. Comprehensive evaluations show that Lever reduces inference latency by an average of 2.93x over baseline flash-offloaded inference and 1.50x over conventional speculative decoding, narrowing the latency gap between flash-backed and memory-resident LLM inference.

</details>


### [64] [The Unlearnability Phenomenon in RLVR for Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16787)
*Yulin Chen,He He,Chen Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了RLVR训练中一个反直觉现象：即使模型能生成正确推理路径，仍有大量困难样本无法被学会。通过跨样本梯度分析发现，这些"不可学习"样本存在表征缺陷，表现为与其他样本梯度相似度低且推理模式不可泛化，而现有优化、采样和数据增强方法均无法解决该问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RLVR已被证明能提升LLM的推理能力，但其学习动力学尚未被充分探索。作者发现了一个反直觉现象并希望理解其成因。

Method: 1) 实证揭示不可学习现象的存在；2) 验证现有优化和采样技术无法解决该问题；3) 通过跨样本梯度分析，发现不可学习样本存在表征层面的根本问题；4) 检验数据增强对梯度相似性的改善效果。

Result: 困难样本中存在大量即使有正确rollout也无法被学会的样本；这些样本与其他样本的梯度相似度低，且推理模式不可泛化；数据增强无法改善梯度相似性。

Conclusion: 本研究首次系统刻画了RLVR训练中的不可学习数据现象，揭示了当前RL方法在推理任务上的根本局限性。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) has proven effective in improving Large Language Model's (LLM) reasoning ability. However, the learning dynamics of RLVR remain underexplored. In this paper, we reveal a counterintuitive phenomenon: among hard examples that the model initially struggles with, a substantial subset remains unlearnable even when correct rollouts are present. To understand the phenomenon, we first demonstrate that existing optimization and sampling techniques fail to resolve unlearnability. With cross-example gradient analysis, we show that unlearnable examples have fundamental representation issue, characterized by low gradient similarity with the rest of the examples and ungeneralizable reasoning patterns. We further show that representation flaws are difficult to mitigate in RL, as data augmentation does not improve gradient similarity. Our study provides the first systematic characterization of unlearnable data in RLVR training and reveals fundamental limitations in current RL approaches for reasoning tasks. Code and data are available at \url{https://github.com/yulinchen99/unlearnability-rlvr}.

</details>


### [65] [TIER: Trajectory-Invariant Execution Rewards for Multi-Step Tool Composition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16790)
*Anay Kulkarni,ChiaEn Lu,Dheeraj Mekala,Jayanth Srinivasa,Gaowen Liu,Jingbo Shang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出TIER（轨迹不变执行奖励）框架，通过函数模式和运行时执行提供密集奖励信号，无需参考轨迹即可训练LLM进行多步工具组合，在DepthBench上实现超90%准确率，而传统方法在4步后失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习方法无法扩展到多步工具组合场景：基于结果的奖励仅提供稀疏反馈，而基于轨迹监督的奖励依赖标注参考解，惩罚有效替代路径且难以扩展。

Method: TIER奖励框架分解为四个层次：格式有效性、模式遵从性、执行成功性和答案正确性，从函数模式和运行时执行中直接推导监督信号，而非参考轨迹。任何有效执行路径均可获得奖励。

Result: 在DepthBench（1-6步组合基准）上，TIER在所有步骤上实现>90%准确率，而轨迹监督方法在4步后崩溃；在BFCL v3和NestFUL上一致提升；消融实验证实所有奖励组件均必要。

Conclusion: TIER通过多层级密集奖励机制有效支持多步工具组合推理，能够自然适应多种解决方案策略和演化的工具接口，相比轨迹监督方法具有显著优势。

Abstract: Tool use enables large language models to solve complex tasks through sequences of API calls, yet existing reinforcement learning approaches fail to scale to multi-step composition settings. Outcome-based rewards provide only sparse feedback, while trajectory-supervised rewards depend on annotated reference solutions, penalizing valid alternatives and limiting scalability. We propose TIER: Trajectory-Invariant Execution Rewards, a reward framework that derives supervision directly from function schemas and runtime execution, rather than from reference trajectories. The reward decomposes into format validity, schema adherence, execution success, and answer correctness, providing dense, interpretable sequence-level feedback derived from fine-grained verification of individual steps of tool use. This design allows any valid execution path to receive credit, naturally supporting multiple solution strategies and adapting to evolving tool interfaces. On DepthBench, a compositional benchmark stratified by depth (1 to 6 steps), TIER achieves >90% accuracy across steps, where trajectory-supervised rewards collapse beyond step-4. We further demonstrate consistent gains on benchmarks like BFCL v3 and NestFUL. Ablation studies confirm that all reward components are necessary, highlighting the importance of multi-level supervision for compositional reasoning.

</details>


### [66] [Cross-Domain Molecular Relational Learning: Leveraging Chemical Structure-Activity Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16799)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分子关系学习方法局限于域内建模，存在域封闭效应，难以解释跨域相互作用机制，亟需跨域分子关系学习框架。

Method: 1）基于子结构拓扑差异的梯度反转策略学习域依赖的分子结构表征；2）跨域表征引导机制对齐源域与目标域的官能团语义信息，学习跨域一致性信息。

Result: 在两种典型跨域策略下，DisTrans在16种基线方法中表现最优，即使在显著域间差异下仍保持良好性能。

Conclusion: DisTrans通过域对抗训练与结构-语义迁移差异优化，有效实现了跨域分子结构与视觉图像的适应性表征学习。

Abstract: Recent advances in molecular representation integrates molecular topological and visual modalities, opening new avenues for precise Molecular Relational Learning (MRL). Existing MRL methods focus on intra-domain modeling, and their inherent domain-closed effect limits applicability to molecular science, particularly in elucidating cross-domain interaction mechanisms. Consequently, the imperative for Cross-Domain Molecular Relational Learning has become increasingly pressing. Benefiting from structure-activity analysis, we propose the Domain Adversarial Training Network with Structural-Semantic Transfer Discrepancy (DisTrans) to optimize cross-domain adaptive representation for molecular structures and visual images. 1) We employ the gradient reversal strategy based on substructure topological discrepancies between domains to learn the domain dependence of molecular structures. This strategy guides the model to adapt to the structural adjacency patterns in the target domain, generating domain-separable structural representations. 2) We apply the cross-domain representation guidance mechanism to align the functional-group semantic information between the source and target domains, learning cross-domain consistency information. The experimental results in two typical cross-domain strategies demonstrate that DisTrans outperforms 16 baseline methods, maintaining satisfactory performance even under pronounced inter-domain discrepancy.

We propose the Affinity-Aligned Multimodal Learning Analytics (AAMLA) framework, whose core contribution is the Cross-modal Affinity-guided Modality Alignment (CAMA) module, which explicitly models inter-modal relationships via affinity matrices and enforces cross-modal consistency through contrastive learning, enabling adaptive suppression of uninformative modalities without discarding them. Method: 提出InGSL（Informative Graph Structure Learning），采用互信息引导的学习策略，在边构建过程中同时考虑节点间的相似性和多样性，作为可插拔模块集成到现有GSL框架中。

Abstract: The quality of graph-structured data is fundamental to the success of modern graph analysis techniques such as Graph Neural Networks (GNNs). Graph Structure Learning (GSL) has emerged as a promising technique that adaptively optimizes node connections. However, we observe that the effectiveness of GSL often comes at the cost of a dramatic expansion in edge count, resulting in significant storage and computational overhead.

*Youngmok Ha,Viktor Schlegel,Yidan Sun,Anil Anthony Bharath*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于雅可比矩阵的任务感知局部差分隐私方法，通过识别任务关键子空间并重塑噪声分布（从各向同性变为各向异性），在保持隐私预算不变的情况下显著提升数据效用，在CIFAR-10-C上使PrivUnit2和PrivUnitG的效用提升约20%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统LDP机制是任务无关的，在所有维度上均匀注入噪声，导致数据效用严重下降。需要一种能够在保持隐私保证的同时，根据下游任务需求差异化处理噪声的方法。

Method: 利用公开下游模型的雅可比矩阵识别任务关键子空间，选择性地在关键维度上衰减噪声，将标准LDP的各向同性噪声重塑为各向异性分布，同时保持每个维度的隐私预算统一。

Conclusion: 该方法通过任务导向的噪声重塑策略，在不牺牲隐私的前提下有效提升了LDP的数据效用，具有良好的普适性和可扩展性。

Abstract: While Local Differential Privacy (LDP) serves as a foundational primitive for distributed data collection, its stringent noise injection requirement often leads to severe degradation in data utility. This degradation stems from the task-agnostic nature of conventional LDP mechanisms, which inject noise uniformly across all dimensions regardless of their relative importance to the downstream objective. To address this issue, we propose a novel approach that mitigates noise in task-relevant subspaces of the data representation. Our method identifies task-critical subspaces via the Jacobian matrix of the public downstream model, selectively attenuates noise along those dimensions, and reshapes the isotropic noise of standard LDP into an anisotropic distribution. This method preserves the uniform per-dimension privacy budget while heterogeneously modulating noise impact across dimensions, thereby substantially enhancing data utility. Furthermore, our approach generalizes to both linear and non-linear models and integrates seamlessly with existing mechanisms. Extensive experiments on CIFAR-10-C (Brightness corruption at the highest severity level 5) demonstrate that integrating our approach improves the utility of PrivUnit2 and PrivUnitG by approximately 20\% at $ε=7.5$. The source code is available at \url{https://github.com/ymha/jacobian-anr-ldp}.

### [70] [Decoupling KL and Trajectories: A Unified Perspective for SFT, DAgger, Offline RL, and OPD in LLM Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16826)
*Anhao Zhao,Haoran Xin,Yingqi Fan,Junlong Tong,Wenjie Li,Xiaoyu Shen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统解耦了LLM知识蒸馏中的两个正交维度——前缀来源（教师/学生）和token级KL方向（正向/反向），发现四种有效目标函数，并通过数学推理实验揭示了精度-熵、质量-计算、精度-稳定性三种权衡，提出了KL混合和熵门控长度课程等实用方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM后训练中知识蒸馏的设计空间尚未被充分理解，尤其是蒸馏与强化学习的交互关系不明确。现有离策略蒸馏和同策略蒸馏隐式耦合了前缀来源和KL方向两个正交选择，但这种耦合并非内在必然，需要解耦研究。

Method: 本文通过序列级KL分解，解耦前缀来源（教师/学生前缀）和token级KL方向（正向/反向），推导出四种有效的蒸馏目标函数。在数学推理任务上进行大规模对比研究，评估这四种目标函数作为独立方法和后续RL初始化的效果，并据此提出KL混合和熵门控长度课程方法。

Result: 揭示了三种关键权衡：KL方向导致精度-熵权衡，前缀来源导致质量-计算权衡，训练长度导致精度-稳定性权衡。KL混合方法表明长序列蒸馏需要足够的正向KL权重以防止熵崩溃和长度膨胀。熵门控长度课程在Avg@k和Pass@k上分别提升3.6和5.8个百分点，同时将平均回复长度减少约3倍。

Conclusion: 本文为设计平衡精度、多样性、计算效率和RL行为的推理蒸馏目标函数提供了理论框架和实践方法，证明了蒸馏与RL的深度融合可以带来显著的性能提升和计算效率改进。

Abstract: Knowledge distillation is central to LLM post-training, yet its design space remains poorly understood, especially alongside reinforcement learning (RL). We show that the prevailing paradigms, off-policy distillation and on-policy distillation (OPD), implicitly couple two orthogonal choices: prefix source and token-level KL direction. This follows from decomposing sequence-level KL over autoregressive response distributions: forward KL pairs teacher prefixes with token-level forward KL, and reverse KL pairs student prefixes with token-level reverse KL. We argue this coupling is not intrinsic: decoupling the two axes yields four valid objectives. We establish gradient-level identities showing forward KL gives SFT-style cross-entropy matching with teacher soft targets, whereas reverse KL gives an RL-style policy-gradient objective with a dense teacher-student log-ratio reward, connecting them to off-policy SFT, DAgger-style on-policy SFT, offline-RL-style distillation, and OPD. We conduct an extensive controlled study on math reasoning, evaluating the four objectives both as standalone methods and as initializations for subsequent RL. The results reveal three tradeoffs: KL direction induces an accuracy-entropy tradeoff, prefix source a quality-compute tradeoff, and training length an accuracy-stability tradeoff. Motivated by these findings, we propose KL mixing and an entropy-gated length curriculum. KL mixing shows long-sequence distillation requires substantial forward-KL weight to prevent entropy collapse and length inflation without sacrificing accuracy. The entropy-gated length curriculum improves Avg@k and Pass@k by 3.6 and up to 5.8 points, and cuts average response length by roughly 3x versus fixed long-horizon training. Our results provide a framework and practical methods for designing reasoning distillation objectives that balance accuracy, diversity, compute, and RL behavior.

### [71] [PhysioSeq2Seq: A Hybrid Physiological Digital Twin and Sequence-to-Sequence LSTM for Long-Horizon Glucose Forecasting in Type 1 Diabetes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16860)
*Phat Tran,Neville Mehta,Clara Mosquera-Lopez,Robert H. Dodier,Lizhong Chen,Peter G. Jacobs*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PhysioSeq2Seq是一种混合架构，通过将患者特异性生理建模（ODE数字孪生）与序列到序列LSTM结合，并采用孪生匹配选择最佳生理模型，同时利用内部状态变量作为外生协变量注入编解码器，避免了递归误差累积，在240分钟预测窗口上实现了39.28 mg/dL的MAE，比递归LSTM减少偏差13.89 mg/dL，比纯ODE数字孪生减少MAE 28.62 mg/dL。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准递归LSTM在长时域预测中存在系统性负偏差（误差累积），而纯机械性ODE模型在群体水平参数化时无法跨个体泛化，亟需一种结合两者优势的混合方法用于1型糖尿病长时域血糖预测。

Method: 混合架构PhysioSeq2Seq：对每个血糖片段，通过孪生匹配从300个参数化数字孪生群体中搜索最佳匹配生理模型，将其10个内部ODE状态变量作为外生协变量注入Seq2Seq LSTM的编码器和解码器，采用同步48步预测策略替代递归预测。

Result: 在T1DEXI数据集（348训练+74测试）上，240分钟预测窗口MAE为39.28 mg/dL，平均误差为-10.62 mg/dL；相比递归LSTM减少偏差13.89 mg/dL，相比ODE数字孪生减少MAE 28.62 mg/dL。

Conclusion: 消除架构反馈回路并注入患者匹配的生理状态，是1型糖尿病长时域血糖预测中有效且具有临床意义的策略。

Abstract: Accurate long-horizon glucose forecasting is critical for automated insulin delivery systems, which help people with type 1 diabetes (T1D) manage their glucose and avoid dangerous hypoglycemia. However, standard recursive long short-term memory (LSTM) networks suffer from systematic negative bias at longer horizons due to error compounding, while purely mechanistic ordinary differential equation (ODE) models fail to generalize across individuals when parameterized at the population level. We propose PhysioSeq2Seq, a hybrid architecture that combines patient-specific physiological modeling with a sequence-to-sequence (Seq2Seq) LSTM. For each glucose segment, twin matching searches a population of 300 parameterized digital twins to identify the best-fitting physiological match from a 3-hour continuous glucose monitoring (CGM) history. The 10 internal ODE state variables of the matched twin are injected as exogenous covariates into both the encoder and decoder of the Seq2Seq LSTM. This simultaneous 48-step prediction strategy eliminates recursive error compounding, while the ODE features provide a physics-grounded constraint that bounds long-horizon drift within physiologically plausible ranges. PhysioSeq2Seq was trained on CGM and insulin data from 348 participants in the Type 1 Diabetes Exercise Initiative (T1DEXI) dataset and evaluated on 74 held-out participants. At the 240-minute horizon, PhysioSeq2Seq achieves a mean absolute error of 39.28 mg/dL and a mean error of -10.62 mg/dL, reducing bias by 13.89 mg/dL over the recursive LSTM and reducing mean absolute error by 28.62 mg/dL over the ODE-based digital twin. These results show that eliminating architectural feedback and injecting patient-matched physiological states is an effective and clinically meaningful strategy for long-horizon glucose forecasting in T1D.

To ensure continuous learning, we introduce Memory-Augmented Self-Evolution (MASE), which is a training pipeline that adopts the data collected by TTME to stabilize and enhance the agent's foundational policy. Method: 提出ArtifactLinker两阶段框架：第一阶段使用GNN或图增强LLM对未观测到的模型-数据集链接进行排序；第二阶段通过基于LLM智能体的编码实验验证排名靠前的链接。

Abstract: Scientific artifacts such as models and datasets are foundations for research. With the rapid growth of platforms like HuggingFace, researchers now have access to a large number of artifacts. Yet, a key challenge remains: how can we automatically discover the state-of-the-art (SOTA) model for a given dataset by fully leveraging existing artifacts? We formalize this task as automatic SOTA discovery by modeling HuggingFace as an artifact graph, where nodes are models/datasets and edges represent evaluations. We propose ArtifactLinker, a two-stage framework: (1) ranking promising unobserved model--dataset links using Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) or graph-augmented Large Language Models (LLMs), and (2) verifying top-ranked links via coding experiments with LLM-based agents. We further introduce a benchmark named ArtifactBench with 14,053 artifacts and 51,337 relations to evaluate the performance of both stages.   <summary>Details</summary>

We propose Adversarial Information Masking (AIM), a saliency-guided adversarial feature replacement framework for evaluating both saliency-map faithfulness and masking-operator reliability. AIM replaces selected features with values from an adversarial counterpart of the input and compares degradation under complementary masking orders. We assess reliability using random-attribution bias and stability of explanation-method faithfulness rankings. ### [75] [Decision-Aware Proximal Bridge Learning for Optimal Treatment Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16989)
*Tomàs Garriga,Alejandro Almodóvar,Axel Brando,Gerard Sanz,Eduard Serrahima de Cambra,Juan Parras*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对连续动作空间下存在隐混淆的个体化治疗选择问题，提出了一种决策感知的加权桥损失函数，通过强调决策相关区域来优化治疗选择，并证明了其遗憾界，实验表明该方法能有效降低决策遗憾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有近端因果推断方法主要聚焦于治疗效果和潜在结果估计，而非治疗选择与最优决策；同时，全局因果响应面估计在标准目标函数下会根据观测治疗分布分配建模努力，而非根据决策相关区域，导致次优决策。

Method: 提出一种面向策略的加权桥损失函数，强调决策相关治疗区域同时保持全局稳定性；证明该加权损失通过加权病态常数控制治疗选择遗憾；将框架实例化为多种决策感知的近端桥求解器，交替进行加权桥估计、响应面投影、策略更新和权重细化。

Result: 理论层面证明了遗憾界；实验层面发现决策感知加权在多种桥求解器上均降低遗憾，表明能改善近端设置下的治疗选择。

Conclusion: 决策感知加权桥损失能有效提升近端因果推断中的治疗选择质量，填补了该领域在最优决策方面的空白。

Abstract: Individualized treatment selection with continuous actions requires accurate causal response estimation in decision-relevant regions, rather than uniformly over the entire action space. Estimating a global causal response surface and then choosing the treatment that maximizes it can therefore be suboptimal, since standard estimation objectives allocate modeling effort according to the observed treatment distribution rather than the regions that determine the optimal decision. While decision-aware approaches have been studied in unconfounded settings, this problem remains underexplored in proximal causal inference, where proxy variables and bridge functions enable identification under suitable assumptions even in the presence of hidden confounding. Despite recent progress, proximal methods have primarily focused on treatment-effect and potential-outcome estimation rather than treatment selection and optimal decision-making. To bridge this gap, we introduce a policy-targeted weighted bridge loss that emphasizes decision-relevant treatment regions while retaining global stabilization. We prove a regret bound showing that the proposed weighted bridge loss controls treatment-selection regret through a weighted ill-posedness constant. We instantiate the framework in decision-aware variants of several proximal bridge solvers, yielding practical algorithms that alternate between weighted bridge estimation, response-surface projection, policy update, and weight refinement. Empirically, we find that decision-aware weighting reduces regret across several bridge solvers, suggesting improved treatment selection in proximal settings.

### [76] [Ranking-Aware Calibration for Reliable Multimodal Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16999)
*Peng Cui,Boyao Yang,Jun Zhu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 Ranking-Aware Calibration (RAC)，一种在强化学习后训练阶段通过排序信号（组内排序损失和干净-损坏配对损失）来校准视觉语言模型置信度的方法，无需额外标注即可同时提升推理准确率和校准性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习后训练虽然提升了视觉语言模型的推理准确率，但模型校准很差：终态正确性奖励无法惩罚高置信度错误，也无法将置信度与视觉证据质量关联起来，尤其在输入被破坏或模糊时，模型仍对错误答案报高置信度。

Method: 提出 RAC 框架，包含两个对比信号：(1) 排序感知组损失：同一 prompt 内，更好的 rollout 获得比更差的 rollout 更高的置信度；(2) 干净-损坏配对损失：当视觉证据退化时，模型置信度应降低。两个损失均无需外部置信度标注，可自然集成于基于组的 RL 后训练中。

Result: 在 Qwen2.5-VL 和 InternVL-3.5 上实验，在六个多模态推理基准（含干净和损坏输入）上，排序感知损失通过区分更好与更差的推理显著提升了任务准确率，配对损坏损失降低了退化输入下的校准误差，两者结合在多数设置下实现了最佳校准和准确率。

Conclusion: RAC 通过引入排序信号监督置信度，无需额外成本即可同时改进准确率和校准，有效弥补了终态奖励在置信度建模上的不足。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning post-training has substantially improved the reasoning accuracy of vision-language models, yet the resulting policies remain poorly calibrated. Terminal correctness rewards provide no gradient that penalizes confident errors more than uncertain ones and no signal that ties confidence to the quality of visual evidence, a gap that becomes especially severe under corrupted or ambiguous inputs where models continue to report high confidence on incorrect answers. We introduce Ranking-Aware Calibration (RAC), a training-time framework that supervises confidence using two comparison signals that group-based RL already produces at no additional labeling cost. The ranking-aware group loss enforces that a better rollout receives higher confidence than a worse one within the same prompt. The clean--corrupted pairwise loss enforces that confidence attenuates as visual evidence degrades. Because the ranking signal forces the policy to distinguish between correct and incorrect reasoning paths, it also reinforces task accuracy beyond what correctness rewards alone produce. Both losses require no external confidence annotations and integrate naturally with group-based RL post-training. We instantiate RAC on Qwen2.5-VL and InternVL-3.5 backbones and evaluate on six multimodal reasoning benchmarks under clean and corrupted inputs. Empirical results show that the ranking-aware loss substantially improves task accuracy by teaching the policy to discriminate between better and worse reasoning, while the pairwise corruption loss reduces calibration error under degraded inputs. Their combination achieves the best calibration across all tested backbones while improving accuracy in the majority of settings.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出“决策点”（forks in the road）假设，通过图分支中的不可判读节点和推理模式等可控案例研究模拟决策点场景，追踪微调动态，并设计针对性数据合成和多样性解码机制进行缓解。

Result: 发现覆盖率收缩与训练数据中决策点场景的普遍性密切相关；通过决策点的针对性数据合成和多样性鼓励的解码机制可部分缓解收缩行为。

Abstract: Recent progress in large language models has led to the emergence of reasoning models, which have shown strong performance on complex tasks through specialized fine-tuning procedures. While these methods reliably improve pass@1 accuracy, prior works have observed that they show a coverage shrinkage behavior, where pass@k degrades relative to the base model. In this paper, we investigate the reasoning shrinkage arise under SFT-based post-training. We hypothesize that this behavior is driven by properties of the fine-tuning data, specifically related to decision points or "forks in the road" scenarios where model faces indecipherable patterns with multiple valid reasoning paths. To test this hypothesis, we design controlled case studies that simulate such decision-point settings, spanning indecipherable nodes in graph branching, and reasoning modes. By tracking post-training dynamics in these settings, we find that the shrinkage phenomenon is tightly correlated with the prevalence of decision-point scenarios in the training data. We also demonstrate that this shrinkage behavior can be partially mitigated through targeted data synthesis design of decision-points, and a more systematic diversity-encouraging decoding mechanism. Our findings identify data-centric factors as a key driver of shrinkage in reasoning models and highlight diversity-aware designs as an effective lever for controlling it.

Method: 提出PPE框架，使用双单类密度估计器（dual one-class density estimators）结合融合文本嵌入（fused text embeddings），并引入校准的弃权区域（calibrated abstain region）处理分布外输入。通过轴分层、多LLM合成数据管道生成医学、金融、法律领域数据。核心检测器为T3+OCSVM，在安全与边界安全数据上训练。

Using an axis-stratified, multi-LLM synthetic data pipeline across medicine, finance, and law, we found that traditional Gaussian Mixture baselines fail on borderline-safe stress tests by focusing on linguistic register rather than content.
  Our proposed T3+OCSVM detector, trained on safe and borderline-safe data, achieves a borderline AUROC of 0.93+ while reducing false positives by 44-55 percentage points and maintaining millisecond latency. Compared to supervised MLP classifiers or 14B-parameter LLM judges, our framework offers superior operational suitability, as the former suffers from high abstention rates and the latter from latency and calibration issues. This methodology provides a robust stress-testing standard for any synthetic-data-trained classifier.

Method: 提出D²Evo框架，每轮迭代中：（1）基于当前求解器能力挖掘中等难度锚点；（2）训练提问者（Questioner）生成适当难度级别的多样问题；（3）联合优化求解器和提问者两个组件，实现渐进式推理能力提升。

Existing methods mitigate this scarcity to some extent by generating training samples. However, these approaches suffer from anchor-free generation, ignoring co-evolution, and difficulty mismatch. To address these issues, we propose D$^2$Evo, a Dual Difficulty-aware self-Evolution RL framework. In each iteration, our method mines medium-difficulty anchors based on the current Solver's capability, trains the Questioner to generate diverse questions at appropriate difficulty levels, and jointly optimizes both components to enable progressive reasoning gains. Extensive experiments demonstrate that D$^2$Evo outperforms existing methods on mathematical reasoning benchmarks with fewer than 2K real mathematical samples, and exhibits strong generalization on general reasoning benchmarks.

### [82] [Scale Determines Whether Language Models Organize Representation Geometry for Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17084)
*Weilun Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Subspace PGA指标，发现语言模型中间层的几何结构显著为预测任务组织，但小模型在训练后期会失去这种组织性，而大模型能保持，揭示了尺度影响表征几何组织方式的新维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具虽能刻画表征空间的几何形状，却无法回答这种形状为何种目标服务。作者希望探究语言模型中间层表征的几何结构是否服务于最终的预测任务。

Method: 提出Subspace PGA指标，度量某层距离结构与解嵌入矩阵W_U读出子空间的对齐程度，并与随机子空间对比。在7个Pythia模型（70M-6.9B）和3个跨家族模型上进行实验。

Result: 中间层几何显著为预测组织（峰值z=9-24），但存在尺度依赖性：小模型（d≤1024）在训练后期逐渐失去组织性，而大模型（d≥2048）始终保持。这是由容量权衡导致的：少数主导方向偏离W_U读出，掩盖而非破坏了底层预测结构，移除这些方向可恢复对齐。

Conclusion: 尺度不仅决定了模型预测能力，还决定了表征几何如何组织以实现预测。谱度量或损失曲线均无法捕捉此差异，说明需要新的评估维度。

Abstract: In language models, what a representation encodes is determined by the geometry of its representation space: distances, not activations, carry meaning. Existing tools characterize the shape of this geometry but do not ask what that shape is organized for. We introduce Subspace PGA, a metric that tests whether a layer's distance structure aligns with the readout subspace of the unembedding matrix $W_U$ more than with random subspaces of equal size. Across seven Pythia models (70M--6.9B) and three cross-family models, intermediate geometry is significantly organized for prediction (peak $z = 9$--$24$), but the degree is scale-dependent: small models ($d \leq 1024$) progressively lose it at late layers during training -- even as loss keeps improving -- while large models ($d \geq 2048$) preserve it throughout. We trace this to a capacity trade-off: a few dominant directions migrate away from $W_U$'s readout, masking rather than destroying the predictive structure beneath, and removing them restores alignment. Neither spectral metrics nor loss curves capture this distinction. Scale thus determines not only how well a model predicts, but how its representation geometry is organized to do so.

### [83] [Mechanism Learning: Prototype-Anchored Mechanism Inference for Scientific Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17091)
*Qian Jiang,Liping Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出机制学习（Mechanism Learning）框架，通过估计当前活跃的局部演化规则而非直接预测状态来进行科学预测，在数据稀缺、长程预测、非平稳动力学等脆弱场景下显著优于直接状态预测及FNO、NODE、LSTM等基线方法。

Method: 将局部时空片段压缩为机制描述子，构建数据驱动的结构化机制空间（机制邻近性反映相似的局部演化规则）；利用原型锚点（prototype anchors）——一组稀疏覆盖局部规则空间的代表性机制——来将估计锚定在观测数据上。

Abstract: Scientific forecasting typically relies on direct state prediction, an approach that grows brittle under data scarcity, extended horizons, non-stationary dynamics, or high-dimensional complexity. While raw state trajectories are highly sensitive in these regimes, underlying local evolution rules often exhibit robust reusability. We introduce mechanism learning, a framework that forecasts future states by estimating the currently active local mechanism. Our method compresses local spatiotemporal fragments into mechanism descriptors, forming a data-driven, structured mechanism space where proximity reflects similar local evolution rules. To ground these estimates in observed data, we utilize prototype anchors, a set of representative mechanisms that sparsely cover the space of local rules. We evaluate this approach on Burgers dynamics, WeatherBench2, and Lorenz96. Empirically, the learned mechanism spaces resist collapse and maintain strong local consistency. Compared to direct prediction and other models including FNO, NODE, LSTM, and reservoir-family methods, our framework demonstrates predictive gains in fragile regimes: it significantly improves switching stability in Burgers dynamics and achieves state-of-the-art performance both under the scarce-data fixed-horizon WeatherBench2 protocol and in intermediate-complexity Lorenz96. Ablation studies and drift diagnostics confirm that these improvements are driven by finite prototype anchoring rather than sheer latent capacity. Together, these results establish mechanism learning as a principled, robust alternative to direct state prediction in forecasting complex systems.

</details>


### [84] [Parallel Recursive LSTM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17108)
*Tristan Gaudreault,Yongyi Mao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出PR-LSTM，一种层次化递归架构，通过平衡计算树上的递归非线性状态组合替代从左到右的递归，将递归并行深度从线性降至对数，同时保留非线性门控状态表示，在形式语言基准上优于标准RNN、LSTM和Transformer基线，且避免了注意力的二次缩放。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer的自注意力机制在处理长序列时面临二次时间和内存开销，而LSTM等递归模型虽具有强状态跟踪能力但严格顺序计算限制了并行性。现有方法（如线性注意力、状态空间模型）往往牺牲表达力（如要求关联性假设）来换取效率。

Method: PR-LSTM采用层次化递归结构：先将token独立映射到隐状态，再通过可学习的门控组合模块在平衡二叉树上递归合并状态。该结构利用并行扫描（parallel scan）中的归约模式作为固定执行调度，而非假设关联性递归，从而在保留非线性门控状态更新的同时将并行深度从O(n)降至O(log n)。

Result: 在形式语言基准上，PR-LSTM解决了比标准RNN、LSTM和Transformer基线更多的任务，展示了强序列长度泛化能力，且避免了注意力机制中的二次缩放开销。

Conclusion: 递归计算可以通过层次化重组来暴露并行性，且无需将转移动态限制为线性或关联形式，为非关联非线性递归的高效并行化提供了新途径。

Abstract: Transformers have become the dominant architecture for sequence modeling by using self-attention to enable expressive and highly parallel processing. However, the resulting quadratic time and memory costs limit efficiency in long-context settings. Recurrent models such as LSTMs provide explicit nonlinear state updates and strong state-tracking capabilities, yet their strictly sequential computation limits parallelism. We introduce the Parallel Recursive LSTM (PR-LSTM), a hierarchical recurrent architecture that replaces left-to-right recurrence with recursive nonlinear state composition over a balanced computation tree. Tokens are first mapped independently to latent states, which are then recursively merged by a learned gated composition block. This structure uses the reduction pattern underlying parallel scans as a fixed execution schedule, rather than assuming an associative recurrence. As a result, PR-LSTM retains nonlinear gated state representations while reducing recurrent parallel depth from linear to logarithmic. Empirically, PR-LSTM achieves strong sequence-length generalization on formal-language benchmarks, solving more tasks than standard RNN, LSTM, and Transformer baselines, while avoiding the quadratic scaling of attention. These results suggest that recurrent computation can be reorganized hierarchically to expose parallelism without restricting the transition dynamics to linear or associative forms.

### [85] [DynMuon: A Dynamic Spectral Shaping View of Muon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17109)
*Fangzhou Wu,Rikhav Shah,Sandeep Silwal,Qiuyi Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出DynMuon，一种动态谱整形方法，通过在训练过程中将谱指数p从正值调度到轻微负值，以替代Muon优化器中固定的极分解更新，从而实现更快的收敛和更低的验证损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Muon优化器通过将更新矩阵的极因子UV^⊤替代SVD分解UΣV^⊤在LLM训练中表现优异，但固定采用p=0（即UV^⊤）可能并非最优。作者希望探索不同谱指数p对训练的影响，并据此设计更优的调度策略。

Method: 提出一类"谱整形"Muon类更新：将更新矩阵M替换为UΣ^p V^⊤。基于损失函数局部曲率、随机梯度噪声和标签噪声以及训练阶段，理论推导了p的选择策略。据此提出DynMuon，在训练过程中将p从正值动态调度到轻微负值。

Result: 实验表明，DynMuon在不同模型规模、架构和训练设置下均持续取得比Muon更低的验证损失，且达到相同目标损失所需步数减少10.6%-26.5%。

Conclusion: 正向p在训练早期通过强调高曲率方向加速信号收缩，轻微负向p在训练后期将更新强度重新分配到仍包含有用训练信号的低曲率方向。动态调度p能兼顾两阶段优势，显著提升训练效率。

Abstract: In recent years, Muon has emerged as the dominant method for training large language models, and transformers more broadly. The essential difference, when compared to standard gradient descent methods, is to replace the usual update matrix $M=UΣV^\top$ with its polar factor $UV^\top$. In this work, we consider a class of Muon-like updates, where we replace the update $M$ with $UΣ^p V^\top$ for some parameter $p$. We call this a "spectral-shaping" operation, and develop a theory of how to pick $p$ which depends on (a) local curvature of the loss function, (b) noise stemming from stochastic gradients and label noise, and (c) training stage. Our theory and experimentation reveal a previously overlooked behavior: positive $p$ helps early by emphasizing high-curvature directions and accelerating signal contraction, while mildly negative $p$ helps later by reallocating update strength toward low-curvature directions that still contain useful training signals. Building on the insight, we propose DynMuon, an efficient dynamic spectral shaping method that schedules $p$ from positive to mildly negative over training. Extensive experiments across model sizes, architectures, and training settings show that DynMuon consistently achieves lower validation loss than Muon, while requiring 10.6-26.5% fewer steps to reach the same target loss.

</details>

### [87] [When Bits Break Recourse: Counterfactual-Faithful Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17160)
*Chaymae Yahyati,Ismail Lamaakal,Khalid El Makkaoui,Ibrahim Ouahbi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现低比特量化在保持预测精度的同时会破坏算法反事实解释（即决策翻转的可操作性），并提出了反事实忠实量化（CFQ）方法，通过在量化过程中保持反事实行为来同时维护精度和可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准量化方法仅关注预测精度，忽略了量化对反事实解释（即改变决策所需的最小扰动）的影响。量化后原本可行的决策翻转可能失效或成本剧增，这种反事实不稳定性对可解释AI构成隐患。

Method: 形式化了量化下反事实灵敏度的三个维度（有效性、成本、方向稳定性），提出两个评估指标：Validity Drop (VD) 和 Counterfactual Recourse Gap (CRG)。提出反事实忠实量化（CFQ），通过教师模型的反事实点进行知识蒸馏，在全局比特预算下联合优化量化参数和混合精度分配。基于间隔分析推导了量化扰动下有界条件下反事实转移的充分条件。

Result: 在Adult、German Credit、COMPAS数据集上，精度匹配的基线方法会显著损害反事实稳定性，而CFQ在保持精度的同时，在不同比特预算下显著改善了VD和CRG指标。

Conclusion: 量化模型的评估不能仅依赖精度指标，需要关注反事实稳定性；所提CFQ方法能有效在精度和可解释性之间取得平衡。

Abstract: Quantization can preserve predictive accuracy under low-bit deployment while silently breaking algorithmic recourse: an actionable change that flips a decision before quantization may fail after quantization, or become substantially more costly. We formalize counterfactual sensitivity under quantization through validity, cost, and direction stability, and introduce two metrics: Validity Drop (VD) and Counterfactual Recourse Gap (CRG) that reveal recourse failures invisible to accuracy. We propose Counterfactual-Faithful Quantization (CFQ), which trains quantizer parameters and mixed-precision bit allocation to preserve counterfactual behavior by enforcing the target outcome at teacher recourse points under a global bit budget. A margin-based analysis gives a sufficient condition for recourse transfer under bounded quantization perturbations. Experiments on Adult, German Credit, and COMPAS show that accuracy-matched baselines can significantly degrade recourse stability, while CFQ maintains accuracy and substantially improves VD and CRG across bit budgets.

### [88] [TriAxialKV: Toward Extreme Low-Precision KV-Cache Quantization for Agentic Inference Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17170)
*Hanzhang Shen,Haoran Wu,Yiren Zhao,Robert Mullins*

As a result, their context exhibits structure that can carry different importance along three key axes: temporal recency to the current turn, modality such as text or image tokens, and semantic role such as user queries, tool calls, observations, or reasoning. These axes capture distinct token behaviors and lead to different sensitivities to KV-cache compression. However, existing KV-cache quantization methods are typically homogeneous or exploit only heterogeneity on a single dimension, such as temporal proximity or modality, overlooking the interactions among them. To this end, we introduce TriAxialKV, a novel mixed-precision KV-cache quantization scheme that assigns each token a triaxial tag, calibrates per-tag sensitivity, and allocates INT2/INT4 bitwidths under a fixed memory budget. ### [90] [The Geometry of Projection Heads: Conditioning, Invariance, and Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17180)

TL;DR: 本文通过将投影头建模为 backbone 表示流形上的可训练黎曼度量，建立了自监督学习中投影头的几何理论。研究表明线性头执行隐式子空间白化，非线性头则通过深度控制能力适应局部度量以满足损失拓扑约束。平滑非线性头在退化平衡点处Hessian本征值天然为负，使其不稳定。实验证明Swish等平滑激活函数可产生显式负曲率以逃离坍塌，而线性/ReLU头则依赖离散优化和BatchNorm。最后从几何角度解释了信息-不变性权衡及必须丢弃头的原因。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 平滑非线性头（如Swish）在连续梯度流下通过固有负曲率机制使坍塌平衡点不稳定，从而逃离维度坍塌；线性头和ReLU头则缺乏此能力，需依赖离散优化和BatchNorm。投影头本质上是通用几何缓冲器，解耦语义主干与预训练目标的刚性约束。

Conclusion: 投影头作为一个可训练的黎曼度量，其作用是充当几何缓冲器，保护backbone表示不被预训练目标的破坏性约束所扭曲。这一几何框架统一解释了投影头的设计与使用规范（如为什么需要非线性、为什么必须丢弃）。

Abstract: We develop a geometric theory of projection heads in self-supervised learning by modeling the head as a trainable Riemannian metric on the backbone representation manifold. We show that linear heads perform implicit subspace whitening, while nonlinear heads adapt local metrics to satisfy the specific topological constraints of the loss, with head depth empirically dictating this capacity. Analyzing dimensional collapse, we prove that smooth nonlinear heads natively induce negative eigenvalues in the Hessian at collapsed equilibria, making them unstable. We empirically validate this by continuously tracking the optimization geometry during training, which reveals that smooth activations like Swish can generate explicit negative curvature to escape collapse, whereas linear and ReLU heads under continuous-time gradient flow cannot, relying instead on discrete-time optimization dynamics and BatchNorm. Finally, we geometrically characterize how metric degeneracy governs the information-invariance trade-off, explaining why the head must be discarded. Evaluated across contrastive and decorrelation-based objectives on foundation models, our results demonstrate that the projection head acts as a universal geometric buffer, decoupling the semantic backbone from the rigid, destructive constraints of the pretraining objective.

To improve efficiency, recent architectures like Point Transformer V3 (PTv3) adopted static serialization methods, such as Hilbert curves or Z-order, to organize unstructured points for window-based attention. However, these fixed orderings are not optimal for capturing the complex geometry of disaster scenes. In this paper, we propose OPTNet (Ordering Point Transformer Network), which introduces a learnable Point Sorter module. OPTNet utilizes a self-supervised ordering loss to dynamically predict an optimal permutation that maximizes the locality of the attention mechanism. We evaluate our method on the 3DAeroRelief dataset, significantly outperforming state-of-the-art baselines.

</details>


### [92] [FishBack: Pullback Fisher Geometry for Optimal Activation Steering in Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17231)
*Sihan Wang,Jiayi Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出FishBack框架，通过将语言模型的激活空间从欧几里得几何修正为基于Fisher信息度量的非欧几何，推导出闭合形式的最优转向方程。实验表明，在GPT-2上该方法的转向效率显著优于CAA、ActAdd、ITI等现有方法，偏离目标KL降低1.3-2.5倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有激活转向方法普遍假设语言模型的激活空间是欧几里得空间，但本文发现该假设严重不成立——模型输出行为诱导的局部Fisher信息度量与欧几里得度量在相对谱范数上偏差超过97%，且有效维度仅为环境空间的2-17%。

Method: 1. 从softmax层的Fisher信息度量出发，通过后续层的Jacobian拉回得到非欧度量。2. 基于该度量推导闭合形式的转向方程，识别任意目标概念的最小畸变方向。3. 提出层间递归分解，揭示CAA、ActAdd、ITI等方法隐式采用近似度量。4. 通过一个谱诊断指标（隐式度量成本与Fisher最优成本之比）定量预测各方法性能差距。

Result: 在GPT-2上，FishBack在三个动词形态概念和四个层上持续优于所有欧几里得基线：偏离目标KL比欧几里得梯度下降低1.3-2.5倍，比CAA在匹配概念概率时低1.5倍。

Conclusion: 语言模型的激活空间本质上是非欧几里得的，Fisher信息度量框架为激活转向提供了理论基础和最优解，且能统一解释和预测现有方法的性能差异。

Abstract: Activation steering methods modify intermediate representations of language models to control output behavior, but universally assume the activation space is Euclidean. We show this assumption fails drastically: the local geometry induced by the model's own output behavior -- the Fisher information metric of the softmax layer, pulled back through the Jacobian of subsequent layers -- deviates from the Euclidean metric by over 97% in relative spectral norm on GPT-2, with an effective dimensionality of only 2--17% of the ambient space. From this pullback Fisher metric, we derive a closed-form steering equation that identifies the minimum-distortion direction for any target concept, yielding a closed-form optimal direction at each point that can be applied iteratively without manifold fitting or data-driven geometry estimation. We call the resulting framework FishBack. The metric admits a layer-wise recursive decomposition, which reveals that existing methods -- CAA, ActAdd, ITI, and others -- each implicitly adopt a particular approximate metric, and that their performance gaps are quantitatively predicted by a single spectral diagnostic: the ratio of their implicit metric's cost to the Fisher-optimal cost. On GPT-2, iterative pullback steering consistently outperforms all Euclidean baselines across three verb-morphology concepts and four layers, with off-target KL reductions of $1.3\times$--$2.5\times$ relative to Euclidean gradient ascent and $1.5\times$ relative to CAA at matched concept probability.

### [93] [Dimension-Free Convergence of Discrete Diffusion Models: Adjoint Equations Induce the Right Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17232)
*Kelvin Kan,Xingjian Li,Benjamin J. Zhang,Tuhin Sahai,Stanley Osher,Markos A. Katsoulakis*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有离散扩散模型的收敛理论存在根本性局限：KL散度分析在奇异先验（如掩码分布）下发散，而总变差（TV）边界依赖于状态空间大小S，在词汇量达数十万的现代语言任务中失效。

Method: 提出了四项关键技术：1) 在可观测量空间通过伴随方程而非直接处理概率测度；2) 正则性分析得到任意IPM的边界；3) 耦合论证消除均匀转移下的S依赖；4) 得分-边缘抵消技术消除掩码转移下的S依赖。

Result: 首次得到完全独立于状态空间大小S的收敛边界，适用于掩码和均匀两种先验，仅需单一标准速率矩阵正则性假设，兼容时间非齐次调度。

Conclusion: 该框架从根本上区别于以往分析，避免了路径空间KL和现有TV方法的缺陷，并为离散扩散模型的理论研究提供了通用工具包。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion has become a leading framework for generative modeling in various applications including language, vision, and biology. Existing convergence theory, however, exhibits fundamental limitations. KL-based analyses diverge under singular priors such as the masked distribution, while bounds in total variation (TV) depend on the state space size $S$ and become vacuous for modern language tasks, where vocabularies contain hundreds of thousands of tokens. We develop a unified adjoint-equation-based framework that establishes dimension-free convergence guarantees in any integral probability metric (IPM). To the best of our knowledge, our bounds are the first to be entirely free of $S$ and applicable to both masked and uniform priors. Importantly, our theory relies only on a single standard rate-matrix regularity assumption and is compatible with time-inhomogeneous schedules.
  Four novel techniques drive our improvements: working in the space of observables via adjoint equations rather than directly with probability measures, a regularity analysis that yields bounds on any IPM, a coupling argument that removes $S$-dependence under uniform transitions, and a score-marginal cancellation technique that removes $S$-dependence under masked transitions. Our framework thus sharply departs from prior analyses and avoids the shortcomings of pathspace-KL and existing TV-based approaches. Beyond convergence bounds, our framework provides a versatile toolkit for further theoretical study of discrete diffusion models.

Abstract: We study the dynamic joint assortment selection and positioning problem, where the attraction of each product depends on both its intrinsic appeal and its display position under a Multinomial Logit (MNL) choice framework. Our study ranges from the multiplicative position effects model, in which each product's attraction is scaled by a position-specific factor, to a general position effects model assigning independent attraction parameters to every product--position pair to capture heterogeneous synergies. For both models, we design round-based learning algorithms that update decisions after every single feedback, and establish the first regret-optimal characterization. Besides, our round-based algorithms provide the prompt operations needed by modern platforms. For the multiplicative model, we develop a cross-position pairwise maximum likelihood estimator with a clipping mechanism, and prove that our algorithm P2MLE-UCB attains a regret of $\tilde{O}(\sqrt{NT})$, matching the lower bound and closing the $\sqrt{K}$ gap left by prior epoch-based analyses. For the general model, we establish a minimax lower bound and propose GP2-UCB with a matching upper bound. Moreover, we design an efficient subroutine for the per-round joint assortment and positioning optimization based on Dinkelbach's method and maximum-weight bipartite matching. Numerical experiments on synthetic data and the Expedia dataset show that our algorithms consistently outperform state-of-the-art benchmarks.

### [96] [Fidelity Probes for Specification--Code Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17246)
*Ferhat Erata,Hao Zhou,Luke Huan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出**忠诚度探针（fidelity probes）**，即从参考工件（如代码）自动生成的自然语言问题及其真实答案，用于评估候选规约（specification）的准确性。忠诚度（fidelity）定义为探针一致的比例，可分解为矛盾率和覆盖缺口率，驱动有针对性的规约编辑直至收敛。在含15个程序、约12k行COBOL的基准（AWS CardDemo）上，经8轮迭代将冻结测试规约忠诚度从0.63提升至0.94，且仅用4轮速率数据即可通过两状态马尔可夫不动点$F^\dagger$预测收敛位置。探针来源包括LLM读取代码或基于控制流、数据流及系统依赖图的静态分析管道（可调混合比例）。使用冻结留出集的探针重采样协议提供Hoeffding界下的过拟合判别指标，实测训练/测试差距比该界限低一个数量级以上。三种图基混合方案将忠诚度提升+16至+30点；跨分布评估表明LLM与符号通道具有互补性。在五个独立LLM家族（Anthropic、DeepSeek、Google、Alibaba、OpenAI）上的跨族生成器扫描证实收敛行为不依赖于单一模型族：五个非Claude生成器中有三个的轨迹与马尔可夫不动点预测一致，而冻结测试协议主动证伪了探针分布随迭代漂移的两个生成器。该方法适用于任何应描述相同行为的工件对。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有规约（specification）与代码实现之间的一致性验证缺乏系统化、可量化的自动评估方法，尤其是当规约以自然语言形式存在时，难以准确度量其与实际代码行为的对齐程度。

Method: 1) 从参考工件（代码）自动生成自然语言探针问题及真实答案；2) 在候选规约中回答这些探针，计算忠诚度（一致比例）；3) 将忠诚度分解为矛盾率和覆盖缺口率，驱动针对性规约编辑；4) 使用两状态马尔可夫模型预测收敛不动点；5) 探针可来自LLM或基于图的静态分析（控制流图、数据流图、系统依赖图），支持可调混合；6) 采用冻结留出集的探针重采样协议进行过拟合判别。

Result: 在15程序、约12k行COBOL基准上，冻结测试规约忠诚度从0.63提升至0.94（8轮迭代）；仅需4轮速率数据即可预测收敛位置。图基混合方案提升+16至+30点忠诚度；LLM与符号通道互补。跨五个LLM家族验证，三个生成器轨迹与马尔可夫预测一致，两个被协议证伪。实测训练/测试差距比Hoeffding界低一个数量级以上。

Conclusion: 忠诚度探针是一种有效的、系统化的规约-代码一致性评估与修复方法，具有收敛可预测性、探针来源可组合性、跨模型家族通用性，且过拟合风险极低。该方法可推广至任何应描述相同行为的工件对。

Abstract: We introduce fidelity probes: natural-language questions generated from a reference artifact with code-derived ground-truth answers, answered from a candidate specification. The fraction of agreeing probes, which we call the fidelity, decomposes into contradiction and coverage-gap rates that drive targeted spec edits to convergence. On a 15-program, roughly 12k-line COBOL benchmark (AWS CardDemo), we raise frozen-test specification fidelity from 0.63 to 0.94 over eight iterations, with the plateau location predicted by a two-state Markov fixed point $F^\dagger$ from just four iterations of rate data. Probes come from an LLM reading the code or from a static-analysis pipeline over its control-flow, data-flow, and system-dependence graphs, with a tunable mixture. A probe-resampling protocol with a frozen held-out set gives a Hoeffding-bounded overfitting discriminant; our measured train/test gap stays more than an order of magnitude below this envelope. Three graph-grounded mixtures lift fidelity by +16 to +30 points; cross-distribution evaluation shows the LLM and symbolic channels are empirically complementary. A cross-family generator sweep on five independent LLM lineages (Anthropic, DeepSeek, Google, Alibaba, OpenAI) confirms the convergence behaviour is not tied to any single model family: three of five non-Claude generators produce trajectories consistent with the Markov fixed-point prediction, and the frozen-test protocol actively falsifies the two generators whose probe distributions drift across iterations. The method applies to any pair of artifacts that are supposed to describe the same behaviour.

Abstract: This work introduces a general framework for calibeating based on regret minimization. Technically, our results for the family of Tsallis losses that we consider are U-calibration results, simultaneously obtaining logarithmic regret for all losses in this family while having a weaker dependence on the dimension compared to previous results. Of potential independent interest, we also show a new regret equality for the regret of Be The Regularized Leader. ### [99] [State-of-the-Art Claims Require State-of-the-Art Evidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17273)
*YongKyung Oh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了AI/ML研究中广泛存在的"声明-证据鸿沟"：基准测试中声称SOTA的模型，其平均分优势往往缺乏效应量、一致性和鲁棒性支持。对10个跨领域基准的分析表明，超过一半的顶级模型比较中至少有一项SOTA隐含假设不成立，聚合增益常由异常数据集驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI/ML研究中广泛使用SOTA声明，但这些声明往往仅基于基准测试的聚合得分排名，缺乏充分证据支持。作者旨在识别并量化这种声明与证据之间的差距，推动更严谨的科研实践。

Method: 作者分析了10个跨领域公共基准排行榜中顶级模型之间的比较，检验SOTA声明隐含的三个关键属性是否成立：有意义的效应量、跨任务的一致性、以及移除数据集后的鲁棒性。

Result: 超过一半的顶级模型比较中，至少有一个SOTA隐含属性不成立。聚合得分的提升常常由少数异常数据集驱动，而非模型在大多数任务上的普遍优越性。即使任务数量较多的基准测试中，这一脆弱性依然存在。

Conclusion: 研究结论认为，声明语言应与证据强度相匹配。作者呼吁更诚实的报告方式，不需要额外的实验，只需如实反映结果实际揭示的内容，从而实现模型间更精确和可解释的比较。

Abstract: State-of-the-Art (SOTA) claims pervade Artificial Intelligence (AI) and Machine Learning (ML) research. These claims rest on benchmark evaluations, where models are ranked by aggregate scores across tasks. Public benchmarks or leaderboards are the most visible instance, but the same structure appears in paper tables throughout the literature. However, such minimal evidence often cannot support these strong claims. We identify a widespread claim-evidence gap in AI benchmarking. Claiming SOTA carries implicit assumptions beyond mean score superiority, suggesting that a model meaningfully outperforms alternatives across most tasks. However, a marginal improvement in the mean score merely indicates a top average rank rather than true superiority. Analyzing ten cross-domain benchmarks from public leaderboards, we found that in more than half of top-model comparisons, at least one commonly assumed property of superiority does not hold. These properties include meaningful effect size, consistency across tasks, or robustness to dataset removal. Instead, aggregate gains are frequently driven by outlier datasets. This fragility persists even in benchmarks with many tasks. We argue that claim language should reflect the strength of the underlying evidence. This requires no additional experiments, only honest reporting of what results actually show, enabling more precise and interpretable comparisons across models.

</details>


### [100] [How Do Electrocardiogram Models Scale?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17276)
*Jiawei Li,Fabio Bonassi,Ming Jin,Stefan Gustafsson,Johan Sundström,Thomas B. Schön,Antônio H. Ribeiro*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了心电图（ECG）模型中的神经缩放定律和损失缩放定律。通过在CODE数据集上预训练超过120个模型（参数从20K到200M），解耦了模型架构（ResNet vs Transformer）和预训练范式（监督学习SL vs 自监督学习SSL）的影响。发现：SL模型在分布内存在数据瓶颈，而SSL模型在模型和数据规模上都能稳健扩展；在分布外泛化中，ResNet比Transformer参数效率高1.3-2.5倍，SSL比SL数据效率高16倍、迁移效率高7.6倍；整体上ResNet+SSL组合在未见临床任务上表现最优，但大规模下自监督Transformer开始超越。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缩放定律在自然语言处理中已建立基本框架，但其在ECG模型中的适用性尚不明确。近期研究发现增加模型规模或预训练数据量并不总能带来一致的性能提升，架构归纳偏置、预训练范式和规模提升之间的确切关系尚未被解答。

Method: 在CODE数据集（230万条记录）上预训练超过120个模型（参数从2万到2亿），系统解耦模型架构（ResNet vs Transformer）和预训练范式（监督学习SL vs 自监督学习SSL）的影响，分别研究神经缩放定律和损失缩放定律。

Result: (i) SL模型在分布内存在数据瓶颈，SSL模型在模型和数据规模上均能稳健扩展；(ii) 分布外泛化中，ResNet参数效率比Transformer高1.3-2.5倍，SSL数据效率比SL高16倍、迁移效率高7.6倍；(iii) ResNet+SSL在未见临床任务上整体最优，但超大规模下自监督Transformer开始超越。

Conclusion: 通向有效ECG基础模型的路径在于架构与范式的战略对齐，而非盲目扩大规模。

Abstract: While scaling laws have established a fundamental framework for foundation models in natural language processing, their applicability to electrocardiogram (ECG) models remains poorly characterized. Indeed, recent studies do not always yield consistent downstream gains as one increases the model size or pre-training dataset size of ECG models, leaving the exact roles of architectural inductive biases, pre-training paradigms, and expected improvements with size largely unanswered. In this work, we systematically investigate neural and loss-to-loss scaling laws within the ECG domain. By pre-training over $120$ models (ranging from $20$K to $200$M parameters) on the large-scale CODE dataset ($2.3$M records), we decouple the effects of model architecture (ResNet vs. Transformer) and pre-training paradigm, namely supervised learning (SL) versus self-supervised learning (SSL). We found that (i) SL models are data-bottlenecked in-distribution, whereas SSL models scale robustly across both model and data sizes; (ii) for out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization, ResNets are $1.3$ to $2.5$ times more parameter-efficient than Transformers, while SSL is up to $16$ times more data-efficient and achieves up to $7.6$ times higher transfer efficiency than SL on unseen clinical tasks; (iii) across the observed scales, ResNet-based models generally achieve the lowest OOD loss, with SSL dominating on unseen clinical tasks and self-supervised Transformers overtaking at very large model sizes. Our results suggest that the path to effective ECG foundation models lies in the strategic alignment of architecture and paradigm rather than brute-force scaling.

Abstract: Unstructured sparsity is now natively accelerated by recent GPU kernels and dataflow hardware, shifting the bottleneck from inference execution to the pruning algorithm. End-to-end alternatives such as MaskLLM and PATCH show that learnable masks can close this gap, but their categorical-over-patterns parameterization scales with the number of valid masks per row and does not port to the unstructured setting. ### [103] [Step-wise Rubric Rewards for LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17291)
*Weichu Xie,Haozhe Zhao,Wenpu Liu,Yongfu Zhu,Liang Chen,Minghao Ye,Zirong Chen,Yuqi Xu,Shuai Dong,Ziyue Wang,Xinbo Xu,Kean Shi,Ruoyu Wu,Xiaoying Zhang,Wenqi Shao,Baobao Chang,Nan Duan,Jiaqi Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出步级评分奖励框架（SRaR），通过将评分项归因到具体推理步骤、跨轨迹归一化以及解耦优势估计，解决了基于评分奖励方法中多标准信息丢失、正误步骤统一监督和奖励黑客三大问题，在数学推理任务上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）仅奖励最终答案正确性，缺乏对中间步骤的监督；基于评分的方法（如RaR）虽引入结构化评分，但将多维评分聚合为单一标量应用于整个回答，导致多标准信息丢失、正确与错误步骤被统一监督、以及通过无界自我修正实现奖励黑客等三个缺陷。

Method: SRaR包含三个核心组件：(i) 利用LLM裁判将每个评分项归因到具体推理步骤；(ii) 跨轨迹归一化每步评分，仅对质量有差异的步骤产生学习信号；(iii) 通过解耦优势估计器将步级奖励与结果奖励结合，保持结果基线的稳定性。此外，通过对比蒸馏从强模型中正确与错误推理路径中构建了16K问题的评分数据集。

Result: 在六个数学推理基准上，SRaR在Qwen3-8B上平均准确率提升3.57个百分点，在Qwen3-32B上提升2.75个百分点；AIME 2025上的忠实推理率从34.5%提升至46.7%；自我修正循环从48.1%降低至26.5%。

Conclusion: 步级评分奖励框架（SRaR）通过细粒度的步级监督有效提升了推理质量与忠实度，显著缓解了奖励黑客问题，验证了在强化学习中引入结构化步骤级监督的有效性。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) is widely used to improve reasoning in large language models, but rewards only final-answer correctness with no supervision over intermediate steps. Rubric-based methods such as Rubrics as Rewards (RaR) introduce finer-grained supervision by scoring rollouts against structured criteria, yet the rubric scores are still aggregated into a single scalar applied to the entire response, causing three weaknesses: loss of multi-criterion structure, uniform supervision of correct and incorrect steps, and reward hacking through unbounded self-correction. On 1,000 problems, we find 18.2% of steps in correct-answer responses are wrong yet positively rewarded, while 49.9% of steps in incorrect-answer responses are correct yet penalized. We introduce Step-wise Rubrics as Rewards (SRaR), an RLVR framework that (i) uses an LLM judge to attribute each rubric item to a specific reasoning step, (ii) normalizes per-step rubric scores across rollouts so only steps whose quality varies produce a learning signal, and (iii) combines the per-step reward with the outcome reward through a decoupled advantage estimator that keeps the outcome baseline stable. We further build a 16K-problem rubric dataset by contrastively distilling rubric items from correct and flawed reasoning paths sampled from a strong model. Across six mathematical reasoning benchmarks, SRaR improves average accuracy over RaR by 3.57 points on Qwen3-8B and 2.75 points on Qwen3-32B, raises the Faithful Reasoning Rate on AIME 2025 from 34.5% to 46.7%, and reduces self-correction looping from 48.1% to 26.5%.

### [104] [DISA: Offline Importance Sampling for Distribution-Matching LLM-RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17295)
*Shaobo Wang,Yujie Chen,Yafeng Sun,Wenjie Qiu,Zhihui Xie,Sihang Li,Yucheng Li,Huiqiang Jiang,Xingzhang Ren,Xuming Hu,Dayiheng Liu,Linfeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DISA将分布匹配RL中的配分函数估计与策略学习解耦，通过离线重要性采样预先估计配分函数，在数学和代码基准上优于在线耦合方法和奖励最大化方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分布匹配强化学习方法需要在策略学习的同时在线估计配分函数，导致校准误差直接扭曲策略更新且无法独立诊断。作者希望将配分函数估计移出强化学习循环，实现两者的严格分离。

Method: DISA（解耦重要性采样锚定）方法：离线生成提议轨迹，通过重要性采样估计配分函数，在策略优化前固定该估计值。这实现了配分函数估计与策略学习在数据、梯度、损失和诊断上的完全解耦。

Result: 在6个数学和3个代码基准上，DISA匹配或超过在线耦合基线FlowRL，优于奖励最大化基线GRPO和GSPO，比LoRASFT蒸馏高出最多13.8 Mean@8分。LLM评判器评估显示DISA保留了更多策略级多样性。

Conclusion: 将配分函数估计与策略学习解耦是可行且有效的，能提升分布匹配RL的性能和可诊断性。提议强度和逆温度的敏感性实验遵循了分析预测的偏差-方差模式。

Abstract: Modern reasoning agents are increasingly evaluated on their ability to generate multiple valid solution paths, plans, or tool-use traces for a given input. Standard reward-maximizing RL tends to collapse onto the most easily reinforced high-reward mode, whereas distribution-matching RL aims to allocate probability mass across the entire reward-shaped solution set. Achieving this objective requires computing a prompt-dependent partition function over the trajectory space. Because existing distribution-matching methods learn this partition function online alongside the policy, calibration errors in the partition function directly distort policy updates and remain impossible to diagnose independently. We introduce DISA, short for Decoupled Importance-Sampled Anchoring, which moves this calibration problem outside the RL loop. DISA draws proposal trajectories offline, estimates the partition function via importance sampling, and freezes the resulting partition-function estimate before policy optimization begins. This decoupling preserves the distribution-matching objective while strictly separating partition-function estimation from policy learning in data, gradients, loss, and diagnostics. Empirically, on two open-weight backbones across six math and three code benchmarks, DISA matches or exceeds the online-coupled distribution-matching baseline FlowRL, outperforms rewardmaximization baselines GRPO and GSPO on math averages, and exceeds LoRASFT distillation by up to 13.8 Mean@8 points on the same offline trajectories. An LLM-as-judge evaluation further shows that DISA retains substantially more strategy-level diversity than reward-maximization baselines, and sensitivity studies on the proposal strength and inverse temperature follow the bias-variance pattern predicted by the analysis.

### [105] [Leveraging Error Diversity in Group Rollouts for Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17333)
*Wenpu Liu,Yuqi Xu,Weichu Xie,Yongfu Zhu,Shuai Dong,Ziyue Wang,Wenqi Shao,Xiaoying Zhang,Tong Yang,Nan Duan,Jiaqi Wang*

TL;DR: 本文提出EDAS方法，通过利用组内错误多样性信号来改进基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR），在多个基准测试上取得一致提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR方法对每个prompt采样多条响应并分配二元奖励，但忽略了组输出中错误分布的结构性信息。实证分析发现错误多样性是训练成功的强预测因子，同质化失败的问题从RLVR中获益较少。

Method: 提出错误多样性优势塑形（EDAS），一种轻量级、算法无关的后验调整技术，根据组内错误多样性调节错误rollout的优势信号：放大对主导重复错误的惩罚，减弱对罕见探索性错误的惩罚，从而鼓励模型保持多样化推理路径。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) typically samples multiple responses per prompt and assigns binary rewards based on individual correctness, yet the collective structure of the group output, specifically the distribution of errors, is largely discarded. We identify this as a missed opportunity: empirical analysis reveals that error diversity within a group is a strong predictor of training success, with problems eliciting diverse wrong answers benefiting substantially more from RLVR than those producing homogeneous failures. Motivated by this observation, we propose Error Diversity Advantage Shaping (EDAS), a lightweight, algorithm-agnostic technique that modulates the advantage signal for incorrect rollouts based on intra-group error diversity. EDAS amplifies penalties for dominant, repeated errors and attenuates penalties for rare, exploratory ones, thereby encouraging the model to maintain diverse reasoning paths and discouraging error perseveration. Crucially, EDAS operates as a simple post-hoc adjustment that can be seamlessly integrated into any RLVR algorithm. We validate EDAS on top of several mainstream RLVR methods across a series of models and seven challenging math benchmarks, demonstrating consistent improvements. Notably, EDAS yields an average improvement of 6.29 points over DAPO on Qwen3-8B across seven benchmarks, confirming that exploiting the latent information in group rollouts is a broadly effective strategy for strengthening RLVR.

### [106] [Olivia: Harmonizing Time Series Foundation Models with Power Spectral Density](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17340)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Harmonizer模块，通过重塑谱结构隐式协调不同数据集的PSD，理论上对应二阶时间相关性的共享重参数化。进一步设计HarmonicAttention，利用紧凑的谐振子集合在低维交互空间中进行自注意力计算。基于这些机制构建Olivia时间序列基础模型。
